<s> there are numerous commercial jpeg offerings , with more popping up every day . </s> <s> I recommend that you not spend money on one of these unless you find the available free or shareware software vastly too slow . </s> <s> in that case , purchase a hardware assisted product . </s> <s> ask pointed questions about whether the product complies with the final jpeg standard and about whether it can handle the jfif file format many of the earliest commercial releases are not and never will be compatible with anyone else s files . </s> <s> 6b if you are looking for source code to work with free , portable c code for jpeg compression is available from the independent jpeg group , which I lead . </s> <s> a package containing our source code , documentation , and some small test files is available from several places . </s> <s> the official archive site for this source code is ftp.uu.net 137.39 . </s> <s> 1.9 or 192.48 . </s> <s> 96.9 . </s> <s> look under directory graphics jpeg the current release is jpegsrc.v4.tar . </s> <s> z . </s> <s> this is a compressed tar file don t forget to retrieve in binary mode . </s> <s> you can retrieve this file by ftp or uucp . </s> <s> if you are on a pc and don t know how to cope with . </s> <s> tar . </s> <s> z format , you may prefer zip format , which you can find at simtel 20 and mirror sites see note above , file msdos graphics jpegsrc4.zip . </s> <s> this file will also be available on compuserve , in the graphsupport forum go pics , library 15 , as jpsrc4.zip . </s> <s> if you have no ftp access , you can retrieve the source from your nearest comp.sources.misc archive version 4 appeared as issues 55 72 of volume 34 . </s> <s> if you don t know how to retrieve comp.sources.misc postings , see the faq article how to find sources , referred to at the top of section 6 . </s> <s> the free jpeg code provides conversion between jpeg jfif format and image files in gif , pbmplus ppm pgm , utah rle , and truevision targa file formats . </s> <s> the core compression and decompression modules can easily be reused in other programs , such as image viewers . </s> <s> the package is highly portable we have tested it on many machines ranging from pcs to crays . </s> <s> we have released this software for both noncommercial and commercial use . </s> <s> companies are welcome to use it as the basis for jpeg related products . </s> <s> we do not ask a royalty , although we do ask for an acknowledgement in product literature see the readme file in the distribution for details . </s> <s> we hope to make this software industrial quality although , as with anything that s free , we offer no warranty and accept no liability . </s> <s> the independent jpeg group is a volunteer organization if you d like to contribute to improving our software , you are welcome to join . </s> <s> 7 what s all this hoopla about color quantization ? </s> <s> most people don t have full color 24 bit per pixel display hardware . </s> <s> typical display hardware stores 8 or fewer bits per pixel , so it can display 256 or fewer distinct colors at a time . </s> <s> to display a full color image , the computer must map the image into an appropriate set of representative colors . </s> <s> this process is called color quantization . </s> <s> this is something of a misnomer , color selection would be a better term . </s> <s> we re stuck with the standard usage though . </s> <s> clearly , color quantization is a lossy process . </s> <s> it turns out that for most images , the details of the color quantization algorithm have much more impact on the final image quality than do any errors introduced by jpeg except at the very lowest jpeg quality settings . </s> <s> since jpeg is a full color format , converting a color jpeg image for display on 8 bit or less hardware requires color quantization . </s> <s> this is true for all color jpegs even if you feed a 256 or less color gif into jpeg , what comes out of the decompressor is not 256 colors , but thousands of colors . </s> <s> this happens because jpeg s lossiness affects each pixel a little differently , so two pixels that started with identical colors will probably come out with slightly different colors . </s> <s> each original color gets smeared into a group of nearby colors . </s> <s> therefore quantization is always required to display a color jpeg on a colormapped display , regardless of the image source . </s> <s> the only way to avoid quantization is to ask for gray scale output . </s> <s> incidentally , because of this effect it s nearly meaningless to talk about the number of colors used by a jpeg image . </s> <s> even if you attempted to count the number of distinct pixel values , different jpeg decoders would give you different results because of roundoff error differences . </s> <s> I occasionally see posted images described as 256 color jpeg . </s> <s> this tells me that the poster a hasn t read this faq and b probably converted the jpeg from a gif . </s> <s> jpegs can be classified as color or gray scale just like photographs , but number of colors just isn t a useful concept for jpeg . </s> <s> on the other hand , a gif image by definition has already been quantized to 256 or fewer colors . </s> <s> a gif does have a definite number of colors in its palette , and the format doesn t allow more than 256 palette entries . </s> <s> for purposes of usenet picture distribution , gif has the advantage that the sender precomputes the color quantization , so recipients don t have to . </s> <s> this is also the disadvantage of gif you re stuck with the sender s quantization . </s> <s> if the sender quantized to a different number of colors than what you can display , you have to re quantize , resulting in much poorer image quality than if you had quantized once from a full color image . </s> <s> furthermore , if the sender didn t use a high quality color quantization algorithm , you re out of luck . </s> <s> for this reason , jpeg offers the promise of significantly better image quality for all users whose machines don t match the sender s display hardware . </s> <s> jpeg s full color image can be quantized to precisely match the user s display hardware . </s> <s> furthermore , you will be able to take advantage of future improvements in quantization algorithms there is a lot of active research in this area , or purchase better display hardware , to get a better view of jpeg images you already have . </s> <s> with a gif , you re stuck forevermore with what was sent . </s> <s> it s also worth mentioning that many gif viewing programs include rather shoddy quantization routines . </s> <s> if you view a 256 color gif on a 16 color ega display , for example , you are probably getting a much worse image than you need to . </s> <s> this is partly an inevitable consequence of doing two color quantizations one to create the gif , one to display it , but often it s also due to sloppiness . </s> <s> jpeg conversion programs will be forced to use high quality quantizers in order to get acceptable results at all , and in normal use they will quantize directly to the number of colors to be displayed . </s> <s> thus , jpeg is likely to provide better results than the average gif program for low color resolution displays as well as high resolution ones ! </s> <s> finally , an ever growing number of people have better than 8 bit display hardware already 15 bit hi color pc displays , true 24 bit displays on workstations and macintoshes , etc . </s> <s> for these people , gif is already obsolete , as it cannot represent an image to the full capabilities of their display . </s> <s> jpeg images can drive these displays much more effectively . </s> <s> thus , jpeg is an all around better choice than gif for representing images in a machine independent fashion . </s> <s> 8 how does jpeg work ? </s> <s> the buzz words to know are chrominance subsampling , discrete cosine transforms , coefficient quantization , and huffman or arithmetic entropy coding . </s> <s> this article s long enough already , so I m not going to say more than that here . </s> <s> for technical information , see the comp.compression faq . </s> <s> this is available from the news.answers archive at rtfm.mit.edu , in files pub usenet news.answers compression faq part 1 3 . </s> <s> if you need help in using the news.answers archive , see the top of this article . </s> <s> 9 what about lossless jpeg ? </s> <s> there s a great deal of confusion on this subject . </s> <s> the jpeg committee did define a truly lossless compression algorithm , I . </s> <s> e . </s> <s> , one that guarantees the final output is bit for bit identical to the original input . </s> <s> however , this lossless mode has almost nothing in common with the regular , lossy jpeg algorithm , and it offers much less compression . </s> <s> at present , very few implementations of lossless jpeg exist , and all of them are commercial . </s> <s> saying q 100 to the free jpeg software does not get you a lossless image . </s> <s> what it does get rid of is deliberate information loss in the coefficient quantization step . </s> <s> there is still a good deal of information loss in the color subsampling step . </s> <s> with the v4 free jpeg code , you can also say sample 1x1 to turn off subsampling . </s> <s> keep in mind that many commercial jpeg implementations cannot cope with the resulting file . </s> <s> even with both quantization and subsampling turned off , the regular jpeg algorithm is not lossless , because it is subject to roundoff errors in various calculations . </s> <s> the maximum error is a few counts in any one pixel value it s highly unlikely that this could be perceived by the human eye , but it might be a concern if you are doing machine processing of an image . </s> <s> at this minimum loss setting , regular jpeg produces files that are perhaps half the size of an uncompressed 24 bit per pixel image . </s> <s> true lossless jpeg provides roughly the same amount of compression , but it guarantees bit for bit accuracy . </s> <s> if you have an application requiring lossless storage of images with less than 6 bits per pixel per color component , you may want to look into the jbig bilevel image compression standard . </s> <s> this performs better than jpeg lossless on such images . </s> <s> jpeg lossless is superior to jbig on images with 6 or more bits per pixel furthermore , jpeg is public domain at least with a huffman back end , while the jbig techniques are heavily covered by patents . </s> <s> 10 why all the argument about file formats ? </s> <s> strictly speaking , jpeg refers only to a family of compression algorithms it does not refer to a specific image file format . </s> <s> the jpeg committee was prevented from defining a file format by turf wars within the international standards organizations . </s> <s> since we can t actually exchange images with anyone else unless we agree on a common file format , this leaves us with a problem . </s> <s> in the absence of official standards , a number of jpeg program writers have just gone off to do their own thing , and as a result their programs aren t compatible with anybody else s . </s> <s> the closest thing we have to a de facto standard jpeg format is some work that s been coordinated by people at c cube microsystems . </s> <s> they have defined two jpeg based file formats jfif jpeg file interchange format , a low end format that transports pixels and not much else . </s> <s> tiff jpeg , aka tiff 6.0 , an extension of the aldus tiff format . </s> <s> tiff is a high end format that will let you record just about everything you ever wanted to know about an image , and a lot more besides . </s> <s> tiff is a lot more complex than jfif , and may well prove less transportable , because different vendors have historically implemented slightly different and incompatible subsets of tiff . </s> <s> it s not likely that adding jpeg to the mix will do anything to improve this situation . </s> <s> both of these formats were developed with input from all the major vendors of jpeg related products it s reasonably likely that future commercial products will adhere to one or both standards . </s> <s> I believe that usenet should adopt jfif as the replacement for gif in picture postings . </s> <s> jfif is simpler than tiff and is available now the tiff 6.0 spec has only recently been officially adopted , and it is still unusably vague on some crucial details . </s> <s> even when tiff jpeg is well defined , the jfif format is likely to be a widely supported lowest common denominator tiff jpeg files may never be as transportable . </s> <s> a particular case that people may be interested in is apple s quicktime software for the macintosh . </s> <s> quicktime uses a jfif compatible format wrapped inside the mac specific pict structure . </s> <s> conversion between jfif and quicktime jpeg is pretty straightforward , and several mac programs are available to do it see mac portion of section 6a . </s> <s> if you have an editor that handles binary files , you can strip a quicktime jpeg pict down to jfif by hand see section 11 for details . </s> <s> another particular case is handmade software s programs gif 2jpg jpg 2gif and image alchemy . </s> <s> these programs are capable of reading and writing jfif format . </s> <s> by default , though , they write a proprietary format developed by hsi . </s> <s> this format is not readable by any non hsi programs and should not be used for usenet postings . </s> <s> use the j switch to get jfif output . </s> <s> this applies to old versions of these programs the current releases emit jfif format by default . </s> <s> you still should be careful not to post hsi format files , unless you want to get flamed by people on non pc platforms . </s> <s> 11 how do I recognize which file format I have , and what do I do about it ? </s> <s> if you have an alleged jpeg file that your software won t read , it s likely to be hsi format or some other proprietary jpeg based format . </s> <s> you can tell what you have by inspecting the first few bytes of the file 1 . </s> <s> a jfif standard file will start with the characters hex ff d8 ff e0 , followed by two variable bytes often hex 00 10 , followed by jfif . </s> <s> 2 . </s> <s> if you see ff d8 at the start , but not the rest of it , you may have a raw jpeg file . </s> <s> this is probably decodable as is by jfif software it s worth a try , anyway . </s> <s> 3 . </s> <s> hsi files start with hsi 1 . </s> <s> you re out of luck unless you have hsi software . </s> <s> portions of the file may look like plain jpeg data , but they won t decompress properly with non hsi programs . </s> <s> 4 . </s> <s> a macintosh pict file , if jpeg compressed , will have a couple hundred bytes of header followed by a jfif header scan for jfif . </s> <s> strip off everything before the ff d8 and you should be able to read it . </s> <s> 5 . </s> <s> anything else it s a proprietary format , or not jpeg at all . </s> <s> if you are lucky , the file may consist of a header and a raw jpeg data stream . </s> <s> if you can identify the start of the jpeg data stream look for ff d8 , try stripping off everything before that . </s> <s> in uuencoded usenet postings , the characteristic jfif pattern is begin line m cx ... whereas uuencoded hsi files will start with begin line m I ... if you learn to check for the former , you can save yourself the trouble of downloading non jfif files . </s> <s> 12 what about arithmetic coding ? </s> <s> the jpeg spec defines two different back end modules for the final output of compressed data either huffman coding or arithmetic coding is allowed . </s> <s> the choice has no impact on image quality , but arithmetic coding usually produces a smaller compressed file . </s> <s> on typical images , arithmetic coding produces a file 5 or 10 percent smaller than huffman coding . </s> <s> all the file size numbers previously cited are for huffman coding . </s> <s> unfortunately , the particular variant of arithmetic coding specified by the jpeg standard is subject to patents owned by ibm , at t , and mitsubishi . </s> <s> thus you cannot legally use arithmetic coding unless you obtain licenses from these companies . </s> <s> the fair use doctrine allows people to implement and test the algorithm , but actually storing any images with it is dubious at best . </s> <s> at least in the short run , I recommend that people not worry about arithmetic coding the space savings isn t great enough to justify the potential legal hassles . </s> <s> in particular , arithmetic coding should not be used for any images to be exchanged on usenet . </s> <s> there is some small chance that the legal situation may change in the future . </s> <s> stay tuned for further details . </s> <s> 13 does loss accumulate with repeated compression decompression ? </s> <s> it would be nice if , having compressed an image with jpeg , you could decompress it , manipulate it crop off a border , say , and recompress it without any further image degradation beyond what you lost initially . </s> <s> unfortunately this is not the case . </s> <s> in general , recompressing an altered image loses more information , though usually not as much as was lost the first time around . </s> <s> the next best thing would be that if you decompress an image and recompress it without changing it then there is no further loss , I . </s> <s> e . </s> <s> , you get an identical jpeg file . </s> <s> even this is not true at least , not with the current free jpeg software . </s> <s> it s essentially a problem of accumulation of roundoff error . </s> <s> if you repeatedly compress and decompress , the image will eventually degrade to where you can see visible changes from the first generation output . </s> <s> it usually takes many such cycles to get visible change . </s> <s> one of the things on our to do list is to see if accumulation of error can be avoided or limited , but I am not optimistic about it . </s> <s> in any case , the most that could possibly be guaranteed would be that compressing the unmodified full color output of djpeg , at the original quality setting , would introduce no further loss . </s> <s> even such simple changes as cropping off a border could cause further roundoff error degradation . </s> <s> if you re wondering why , it s because the pixel block boundaries move . </s> <s> if you cropped off only multiples of 16 pixels , you might be safe , but that s a mighty limited capability ! </s> <s> the bottom line is that jpeg is a useful format for archival storage and transmission of images , but you don t want to use it as an intermediate format for sequences of image manipulation steps . </s> <s> use a lossless format ppm , rle , tiff , etc while working on the image , then jpeg it when you are ready to file it away . </s> <s> aside from avoiding degradation , you will save a lot of compression decompression time this way . </s> <s> 14 what are some rules of thumb for converting gif images to jpeg ? </s> <s> as stated earlier , you will lose some amount of image information if you convert an existing gif image to jpeg . </s> <s> if you can obtain the original full color data the gif was made from , it s far better to make a jpeg from that . </s> <s> but if you need to save space and have only the gif to work from , here are some suggestions for getting maximum space savings with minimum loss of quality . </s> <s> the first rule when converting a gif library is to look at each jpeg , to make sure you are happy with it , before throwing away the corresponding gif that will give you a chance to re do the conversion with a higher quality setting if necessary . </s> <s> some gifs may be better left as gifs , as explained in section 3 in particular , cartoon type gifs with sixteen or fewer colors don t convert well . </s> <s> you may find that a jpeg file of reasonable quality will be larger than the gif . </s> <s> so check the sizes too . </s> <s> experience to date suggests that large , high visual quality gifs are the best candidates for conversion to jpeg . </s> <s> they chew up the most storage so offer the most potential savings , and they convert to jpeg with least degradation . </s> <s> don t waste your time converting any gif much under 100 kbytes . </s> <s> also , don t expect jpeg files converted from gifs to be as small as those created directly from full color originals . </s> <s> to maintain image quality you may have to let the converted files be as much as twice as big as straight through jpeg files would be I . </s> <s> e . </s> <s> , shoot for 1 2 or 1 3 rd the size of the gif file , not 1 4 th as suggested in earlier comparisons . </s> <s> many people have developed an odd habit of putting a large constant color border around a gif image . </s> <s> while useless , this was nearly free in terms of storage cost in gif files . </s> <s> it is not free in jpeg files , and the sharp border boundary can create visible artifacts ghost edges . </s> <s> do yourself a favor and crop off any border before jpeging . </s> <s> if you are on an x windows system , xv s manual and automatic cropping functions are a very painless way to do this . </s> <s> cjpeg s default q setting of 75 is appropriate for full color input , but for gif inputs , q settings of 85 to 95 often seem to be necessary to avoid image degradation . </s> <s> if you apply smoothing as suggested below , the higher q setting may not be necessary . </s> <s> color gifs of photographs or complex artwork are usually dithered to fool your eye into seeing more than the 256 colors that gif can actually store . </s> <s> if you enlarge the image , you will see that adjacent pixels are often of significantly different colors at normal size the eye averages these pixels together to produce the illusion of an intermediate color value . </s> <s> the trouble with dithering is that , to jpeg , it looks like high spatial frequency color noise and jpeg can t compress noise very well . </s> <s> the resulting jpeg file is both larger and of lower image quality than what you would have gotten from jpeging the original full color image if you had it . </s> <s> to get around this , you want to smooth the gif image before compression . </s> <s> smoothing averages together nearby pixels , thus approximating the color that you thought you saw anyway , and in the process getting rid of the rapid color changes that give jpeg trouble . </s> <s> appropriate use of smoothing will often let you avoid using a high q factor , thus further reducing the size of the compressed file , while still obtaining a better looking output image than you d get without smoothing . </s> <s> with the v4 free jpeg software or products based on it , a simple smoothing capability is built in . </s> <s> try smooth 10 or so when converting gifs . </s> <s> values of 10 to 25 seem to work well for high quality gifs . </s> <s> heavy handed dithering may require larger smoothing factors . </s> <s> if you can see regular fine scale patterns on the gif image even without enlargement , then strong smoothing is definitely called for . </s> <s> too large a smoothing factor will blur the output image , which you don t want . </s> <s> if you are an image processing wizard , you can also do smoothing with a separate filtering program , such as pnmconvol from the pbmplus package . </s> <s> however , cjpeg s built in smoother is a lot faster than pnmconvol ... the upshot of all this is that cjpeg quality 85 smooth 10 is probably a good starting point for converting gifs . </s> <s> but if you really care about the image , you ll want to check the results and maybe try a few other settings . </s> <s> for more information about jpeg in general or the free jpeg software in particular , contact the independent jpeg group at . </s> <s> tom lane organizer , independent jpeg group internet bitnet tgl cs.cmu . bitmapped drawings ? </s> <s> let s say you have a scanned image of a line drawing in this case a boat , but it could be anything . </s> <s> on the drawing you have a set of reference points whose adjustments such as stretching contracting uniformly over x or y , or rotating the whole drawing , are not satisfactory . </s> <s> so the question is does any kind soul know of an algorithm for stephen pietrowicz writes ... how do you go about orienting all normals in the same direction , given a set of points , edges and faces ? </s> <s> look for edge inconsistencies . </s> <s> consider two vertices , p and q , which are connected by at least one edge . </s> <s> if p , q is an edge , then q , p should not appear . </s> <s> if both p , q and q , p appear as edges , then the surface flips when you travel across that edge . </s> <s> this is bad . </s> <s> assuming warning ... warning ... warning that you have an otherwise acceptable surface you can pick an edge , any edge , and traverse the surface enforcing consistency with that edge . </s> <s> 0 pick an edge p , q , and mark it as ok 1 for each face , f , containing this edge if more than 2 , oops make sure that all edges in f are consistent I . </s> <s> e . </s> <s> , the face should be p , q , q , r , r , s , s , t , t , p . </s> <s> flip those which are wrong . </s> <s> mark all of the edges in f as ok , and add them to a queue check for duplicates , and especially inconsistencies don t let the queue have both p , q and q , p . </s> <s> 2 remove an edge from the queue , and go to 1 . </s> <s> if a marked edge is discovered to be inconsistent , then you lose . </s> <s> if step 1 finds more than one face sharing a particular edge , then you lose . </s> <s> otherwise , when done , all of the edges will be consistent . </s> <s> which means that all of the surface normals will either point in or out . </s> <s> deciding which way is out is left as an exercise ... kenneth sloan computer and information sciences university of alabama at birmingham 205 934 2213 115a campbell hall , uab station 205 934 5473 fax birmingham , al 35294 1170from steve lamont finding equally spaced points on a sphere . </s> fill me in on what 3do . </s> <s> thanks , bhfrom david watson sphere from 4 points ? </s> <s> in article , edward bolson writes given 4 points non coplanar , how does one find the sphere , that is , center and radius , exactly fitting those points ? </s> <s> finding the circumcenter of a tetrahedron is discussed on page 33 in contouring a guide to the analysis and display of spatial data , by dave watson , pergamon press , 1992 , isbn 0 08 040286 0 , 321p . </s> <s> each pair of tetrahedral vertices define a plane which is a perpendicular bisector of the line between that pair . </s> <s> express each plane in the form ax by cz d and solve the set of simultaneous equations from any three of those planes that have a vertex in common all vertices are used . </s> <s> the solution is the circumcenter . </s> <s> dave watson internet department of mathematics the university of western australia tel 61 9 380 3359 nedlands , wa 6009 australia . </s> <s> fax 61 9 380 1028from steve fortunately . </s> <s> when it died , it died instantly and completely .from henrik harmsen 16 million vs 65 thousand colors andre t . </s> <s> yew writes henrik harmsen writes 1 4 bits per r g b gives horrible machbanding visible in almost any picture . </s> <s> 5 bits per r g b 32768 , 65000 colors gives visible machbanding color gradient picture has almost no machbanding . </s> <s> this color resolution is see some small machbanding on the smooth color gradient picture , but all in all , there are situiations where you get visible mach banding even in a 24 bit card . </s> <s> if you create a very smooth color gradient of dark green white yellow or something and turn up the contrast on the monitor , you will probably see some mach banding . </s> <s> while I don t mean to damn henrik s attempt to be helpful here , he s using a common misconception that should be corrected . </s> <s> mach banding will occur for any image . </s> <s> it is not the color quantization you see when you don t have enough bits . </s> <s> it is the human eye s response to transitions or edges between intensities . </s> <s> the result is that colors near the transistion look brighter on the brighter side and darker on the darker side . </s> <s> andre yeah , of course ... the term mach banding was not the correct one , it should ve been color quantization effect . </s> <s> although a bad color quantization effect could result in some visible mach bands on a picture that was smooth before it was quantizised . </s> <s> henrik harmsen internet chalmers university of technology , sweden . .from peter jackson , ch237a , , where did the hacker ethic go ? </s> <s> from article , by I put it to you thus where has the hacker ethic gone ? </s> <s> if it still exists , where ? </s> <s> and , if it does exist , why are those who call themselves hackers allowing this to perpetuate itself ? </s> <s> why are they not creating new , innovative , interesting ideas to stop the sos from maintaining its choke hold on the computer industry ? </s> <s> since this was posted on comp.ai , I assume there is an ai angle to this . </s> <s> hacking is what ai students do when they re really supposed to be doing something else , e . </s> <s> g . </s> <s> thesis research write up , getting their supervisors pet programs to run properly , etc . </s> <s> no one gets much glory for hacking , and no one gets any money out of it . </s> <s> producing good free software requires an enormous investment of time resources that not many people can , or want to , afford particularly during a recession . </s> <s> in addition , over the last 10 years , I think there has been a de emphasis on producing running programs in ai research , and a greater emphasis on more formal approaches to problem solving . </s> <s> students have been proving theorems instead of writing programs . </s> <s> at a conference a year or two ago , johann de kleer suggested that everyone should get back to the keyboard and write more programs that demonstrate their ideas and I have to say I m inclined to agree . </s> <s> I don t claim to be a superhacker , but I don t think that invalidates my remarks . </s> <s> and I m sure this isn t the whole story . </s> <s> peter jackson , dept of electrical computer eng , clarkson university opinions expressed are not those of my employer or any other </s> <s> ove petter tro , ford fairlane . </s> <s> kongsberg college of engineering , norway email from jonas yngvesson point within a polygon simon crowe writes I am looking for an algorithm to determine if a given point is bound by a polygon . </s> <s> does anyone have any such code or a reference to book containing information on the subject ? </s> <s> well , it s been a while since this was discussed so I take the liberty of reprinting without permission , so sue me eric haines reprint of the very interesting discussion of this topic ... jonas o o x snip snip x o o give a man a fish , and he ll eat one day . </s> <s> give a man a fishing rod , and he ll laze around fishing and never do anything . </s> <s> with that in mind , I reprint without permission , so sue me relevant information posted some years ago on this very problem . </s> <s> note the early use of postscript technology , predating many of this year s papers listed in the april 1st siggraph program announcement posted here a few days ago . </s> <s> eric intersection between a line and a polygon undecidable ? </s> <s> ? </s> <s> , by dave baraff , tom duff newsgroups comp.graphics keywords p , np , jordan curve separation , ursyhon metrization theorem organization program of computer graphics in article ... timothy lyle smith writes I need to find a formula algorithm to determine if a line intersects a polygon . </s> <s> I would prefer a method that would do this in as little time as possible . </s> <s> I need this for use in a forward raytracing program . </s> <s> I think that this is a very difficult problem . </s> <s> to start with , lines and polygons are semi algebraic sets which both contain uncountable number of points . </s> <s> here are a few off the cuff ideas . </s> <s> first , we need to check if the line and the polygon are separated . </s> <s> now , the jordan curve separation theorem says that the polygon divides the plane into exactly two open and thus non compact regions . </s> <s> thus , the line lies completely inside the polygon , the line lies completely outside the polygon , or possibly but this will rarely happen the line intersects the polyon . </s> <s> now , the phrasing of this question says if a line intersects a polygon , so this is a decision problem . </s> <s> one possibility the decision model approach is to reduce the question to some other well known problem q , and then try to solve q . </s> <s> an answer to q gives an answer to the original decision problem . </s> <s> in recent years , many geometric problems have been successfully modeled in a new language called postscript . </s> <s> see postscript language , by adobe systems incorporated , isbn 0 201 1017 9 3 , co . </s> <s> 1985 . </s> <s> so , given a line l and a polygon p , we can write a postscript program that draws the line l and the polygon p , and then outputs the answer . </s> <s> by output , we mean the program executes a command called showpage , which actually prints a page of paper containing the line and the polygon . </s> <s> a quick examination of the paper provides an answer to the reduced problem q , and thus the original problem . </s> <s> there are two small problems with this approach . </s> <s> 1 there is an infinite number of ways to encode l and p into the reduced problem q . </s> <s> so , we will be forced to invoke the axiom of choice or equivalently , zorn s lemma . </s> <s> but the use of the axiom of choice is not regarded in a very serious light these days . </s> <s> 2 more importantly , the question arises as to whether or not the postscript program q will actually output a piece of paper or in other words , will it halt ? </s> <s> now , postscript is expressive enough to encode everything that a turing machine might do thus the halting problem for postscript is undecidable . </s> <s> it is quite possible that the original problem will turn out to be undecidable . </s> <s> I won t even begin to go into other difficulties , such as aliasing , finite precision and running out of ink , paper or both . </s> <s> a couple of references might be 1 . </s> <s> principia mathematica . </s> <s> newton , I . </s> <s> cambridge university press , cambridge , england . </s> <s> sorry , I don t have an isbn for this . </s> <s> 2 . </s> <s> an introduction to automata theory , languages , and computation . </s> <s> hopcroft , j and ulman , j . </s> <s> 3 . </s> <s> the c programming language . </s> <s> kernighan , b and ritchie , d . </s> <s> 4 . </s> <s> a tale of two cities . </s> <s> dickens , c . labs for long enough . </s> <s> by the well known dobbin dullman reduction see j . </s> <s> dullman d . </s> <s> dobbin , j . </s> <s> comp . </s> <s> obfusc . </s> <s> 37 , ii pp . </s> <s> 33 947 , kouhia , . </s> <s> 2 drawing three dimensional objects on a two dimensional screen . </s> <s> the simple answer is , you divide by the depth . </s> <s> for a more verbose explanation , see any of the above references , starting with the foley van dam feiner hughes computer graphics book is certainly a good start . </s> <s> chapter 6 is viewing in 3d , then read chapter 15 , visible surface determination . </s> <s> for more information go to chapter 16 for shading , chapter 19 for clipping , and branch out from there . </s> <s> 3 quantizing 24 bit images down to 8 bits . </s> <s> find a copy of color image quantization for frame buffer display by paul heckbert , siggraph 82 proceedings , page 297 . </s> <s> there are other algorithms , but this one works well and is fairly simple . </s> <s> implementations are included in most raster toolkits see item 7 below . </s> <s> a variant method is described in graphics gems , p . </s> <s> 287 293 . </s> <s> note that the code from the graphics gems series is all available from an ftp site , as described above . </s> <s> check out john bradley s diversity algorithm , which is incorporated into the xv package and described in the back of the manual . </s> <s> the imagemagick package see section 7 for where it is contains another quantizing algorithm which is presented as doing a better job than the other algorithms , but slower . </s> <s> there s also an implementation of wan , wong , and prusinkiewicz , an algorithm for multidimensional data clustering , transactions on mathematical software , vol . </s> <s> 14 2 june , 1988 , pp . </s> <s> 153 162 . </s> <s> avialable as princeton.edu p ub graphics colorquant.shar . </s> <s> this code , in modified form , appears in the utah raster toolkit as well . </s> <s> 4 converting color into grayscale . </s> <s> the ntsc formula is luminosity . </s> <s> 299 red . </s> <s> 587 green . </s> <s> 114 blue 5 quantizing grayscale to black white . </s> <s> the only reference you need for this stuff is digital halftoning , robert ulichney , mit press 1987 , isbn 0 262 2100 9 6 but before you go off and start coding , check out the image manipulation software mentioned in item 7 below . </s> <s> all of the packages mentioned can do some form of gray to b w conversion . </s> <s> 6 rotating a raster image by an arbitrary angle . </s> <s> the obvious but wrong method is to loop over the pixels in the source image , transform each coordinate , and copy the pixel to the destination . </s> <s> this is wrong because it leaves holes in the destination . </s> <s> instead , loop over the pixels in the destination image , apply the reverse transformation to the coordinates , and copy that pixel from the source . </s> <s> this method is quite general , and can be used for any one to one 2 d mapping , not just rotation . </s> <s> you can add anti aliasing by doing sub pixel sampling . </s> <s> however , there is a much faster method , with antialising included , which involves doing three shear operations . </s> <s> the method was originally created for the im raster toolkit see below an implementation is also present in pbmplus . </s> <s> reference a fast algorithm for raster rotation , by alan paeth graphics interface 86 vancouver . </s> <s> an article on the im toolkit appears in the same journal . </s> <s> an updated version of the rotation paper appears in graphics gems see section 1 under the original title . </s> <s> 7 free image manipulation software . </s> <s> there are a number of toolkits for converting from one image . </s> <s> you almost certainly don t need these . </s> <s> read the above item 7 on free image manipulation software . </s> <s> get one or more of these packages and look through them . </s> <s> chances are excellent that the image converter you were going to write is already there . </s> <s> but if you still want one of the format documents , many such files are available by anonymous ftp from zamenhof.cs.rice.edu in directory pub graphics.formats . </s> <s> these files were collected off the net and are believed to be correct . </s> <s> this archive includes pixel formats , and two these is complete , you might want to check both . </s> <s> fits stands for flexible image transport system . </s> <s> it s a file format most often used in astronomy . </s> <s> despite the name , it can contain not only images but other things as well . </s> <s> there is a regular monthly fits basics and information posting on sci.astro.fits read it if you want to know more . </s> <s> 9 converting between vector formats . </s> <s> a lot of people ask about converting from hpgl to postscript , or macdraw to cgm , or whatever . </s> <s> it is important to understand that this is a very different problem from the image format conversions in item 7 . </s> <s> converting one image format to another is a fairly easy problem , since once you get past all the file header junk , a pixel is a pixel the basic objects are the same for all image formats . </s> <s> this is not so for vector formats . </s> <s> the basic objects circles , ellipses , drop shadowed pattern filled round cornered rectangles , etc . </s> <s> vary from one format to another . </s> <s> except in extremely restricted cases , it is simply not possible to do a one to one conversion between vector formats . </s> <s> there is software for converting to and from cgm files on ftp.psc.edu . </s> <s> the contributor states that it runs on unix , ms windows , and possibly the mac . </s> <s> a better , more specific blurb would be most welcome . </s> <s> on the other hand , it is quite possible to do a close approximation , rendering an image from one format using the primitives from another . </s> <s> as far as I know , no one has put together a general toolkit of such converters , but two different hpgl to postscript converters have been posted to comp.sources.misc . </s> <s> check the index on your nearest archive site . </s> <s> a related frequent question is how to convert from some vector format to a bitmapped image from postscript to sun raster format , or hpgl to x11 bitmap . </s> <s> for example , some of the commercial postscript clones for pc s allow you to render to a disk file as well as a printer . </s> <s> also , the postscript interpreters in the next box and in sun s x11 news can be used to render to a file if you re clever . </s> <s> but in general , the answer is no . </s> <s> however , if someone were to put together a vector to vector conversion toolkit , adding a vector to raster converter would be trivial . </s> <s> gnu ghostscript from the fsf current version 2.5 . </s> <s> 2 includes drivers for both ppm and gif format files , thus it can be used as a postscript to ppm or a postscript to gif filter . </s> <s> it implements essentially all of postscript level 1 and alot of display postscript and level 2 . </s> <s> 10 how to get pixar films . </s> <s> the various john lasseter pixar computer animated shorts are available on video tape . </s> <s> you can order them from direct cinema limited film individual price institutional price luxo , jr . </s> <s> 14.95 is , you can t . </s> <s> unless you use a rational spline you can only approximate a circle . </s> <s> the approximation may look acceptable , but it is sensitive to scale . </s> <s> magnify the scale and the error of approximation magnifies . </s> <s> deviations from circularity that were not visible in the small can become glaring in the large . </s> <s> if you want to do the job right , consult the article a menagerie of rational b spline circles by leslie piegl and wayne tiller in ieee computer graphics and applications , volume 9 , number 9 , september , 1989 , pages 48 56 . </s> <s> for rough , non rational approximations , consult the book computational geometry for design and manufacture by I . </s> <s> d . </s> <s> faux and m . </s> <s> j . </s> <s> pratt , ellis horwood publishers , halsted press , john wiley 1980 . </s> <s> for the best known non rational approximations , consult the article good approximation of circles by curvature continuous bezier curves by tor dokken , morten daehlen , tom lyche , and knut morken in computer aided geometric design , volume 7 , numbers 1 4 combined , june , 1990 , pages 33 41 elsevier science publishers north holland 12 how to order standards documents . </s> <s> the american national standards institute sells ansi standards , and also iso international standards . </s> <s> their sales office is at 1 212 642 4900 , send a message to an automated server saying something like send comp.sources.unix fbm , and a few hours or days later you get the file in the mail . </s> <s> in addition , there is at least one ftp by mail server . </s> <s> send mail to saying help and it will tell you how to use it . </s> <s> note that this service has at times been turned off due to abuse . </s> <s> 14 how to tell whether a point is within a planar polygon . </s> <s> consider a ray originating at the point of interest and continuing to infinity . </s> <s> if it crosses an odd number of polygon edges along the way , the point is within the polygon . </s> <s> if the ray crosses an even number of edges , the point is either outside the polygon , or within an interior hole formed from intersecting polygon edges . </s> <s> this idea is known in the trade as the jordan curve theorem see eric haines article in glassner s ray tracing book above for more information , including treatment of special cases . </s> <s> another method is to sum the absolute angles from the point to all the vertices on the polygon . </s> <s> if the sum is 2 pi , the point is inside , if the sum is 0 the point is outside . </s> <s> however , this method is about an order of magnitude slower than the previous method because evaluating the trigonometric functions is usually quite costly . </s> <s> code for both methods plus barycentric triangle testing can be found in the ray tracing news , vol . </s> <s> 5 , no . </s> <s> 3 , available from princeton.edu pub graphics rtnews rtnv 5n3 . </s> <s> z . </s> <s> 15 how to tessellate a sphere . </s> <s> one simple way is to do recursive subdivision into triangles . </s> <s> the base of the recursion is an octahedron , and then each level divides each triangle into four smaller ones . </s> <s> jon leech has posted a nice routine called sphere . </s> <s> c that generates the coordinates . </s> <s> it s available for ftp on ftp.ee.lbl.gov and princeton.edu . </s> <s> is a negative number , the polygon or triangle is clockwise , if positive , it is counterclockwise . </s> <s> from ronald golman s gem in graphics gems ii see section 1 above , area of planar polygons and volume of polyhedra the area of a polygon p0 , p1 , p2 , ... pn , not in the x y plane , is given by area polygon 1 2 n . </s> <s> sigma pk x pk 1 where n is the unit vector normal to the plane and p is a polygonal vertex . </s> <s> the . </s> <s> represents the dot product operator and the x represents the cross product operator . </s> <s> sigma represents the summation operator . </s> <s> that come bundled with a device called the toaster from newtek , inc . </s> <s> that operates on an amiga platform . </s> <s> the lightwave software lightwave lightwave 3d and lightwave modeler allows and artist to create three dimensional photo realistic images for a variety of purposes . </s> <s> why are we doing this ? </s> <s> this mailing list is for those interested in the lightwave software , how it operates and in ideas on how to obtain the best quality images available to them . </s> <s> the list is for those who own the toaster and lightwave as well as those just interested in what can be done with the package . </s> <s> we hope to share information , tips , procedures and to bond as a group . </s> <s> what are the rules ? </s> <s> since lightwave modeler are just a part of the newtek video toaster software , I m sure we will discuss a few items related to the operation of the toaster . </s> <s> however , we will strive to keep the subject revolving specifically around the 3d software , related tools and products . </s> <s> you do not have to own a toaster to join this list ! </s> <s> ok ! </s> <s> how do I join ? </s> <s> to become a member of the lightwave 3d mailing list you must send a mail message to the address in the body of the message enter subscribe lightwave l or just ask to be signed up and I will sign you up to the list . </s> <s> at this point in time the process is manual but I hope to get an automated script based system in place soon . </s> <s> there shouldn t be too much of a delay in joining . </s> <s> expect a welcome message within 5 days after you send your request . </s> <s> then , expect the mail to start flowing in ! </s> <s> how do I post to the list ? </s> <s> contributing to the list is simple . </s> <s> just mail your articles to the following address your article will be processed by the system and distributed to all others joined to the list . </s> <s> your articles will also be sent to you so you know that your article has made it to the list . </s> <s> however , those addresses that are either no good or no longer active will bounce back to you . </s> <s> so , if you post an article and another members address is no longer valid , your original article will be returned to you . </s> <s> this doesn t mean it hasn t been posted to the list . </s> <s> in fact , just the opposite is true . </s> <s> it means that your article was posted and that it couldn t be sent to one or more of the members of the list due to a bad address . </s> <s> note I hope to have a fix for this behavior soon . </s> <s> how do I quit the list ? </s> <s> simply mail a request to be removed from the list to the same address you used to sign up in the body of the message enter unsubscribe lightwave l I will remove your name from the list of members . </s> <s> please , if you join the list and your account is going to be closed or if you will not be able to receive mail for a while , send a request to be removed from the list ! </s> <s> if you are just going to lose access for a short while still send a request for a suspension of your membership and I will suspend forwarding of the articles to you . </s> <s> what about old articles ? </s> <s> I am currently archiving all the articles posted to the list at the originating site bobsbox . </s> <s> however , I can not continue to do this due to lack of disk space . </s> <s> what we need is a volunteer that will maintain a compendium of articles sent to the list . </s> <s> they can compress and store them in archives on their system . </s> <s> they can then periodically post an index of the contents of the compendium and any other information that relates . </s> <s> if there are no volunteers then maybe someone can donate a large scsi hard drive to me for archival purposes . </s> <s> grin I have setup a mail based file server so that anyone interested in the list can obtain information as well as the entire archive of past articles , the membership listing and other information pertaining to the lightwave 3d mailing list . </s> <s> for information on this service , please send a mail message to the first command to the server must be help or user name passwd . </s> <s> use help to request a current copy of the helpfile . </s> <s> use user name passwd to connect to the service . </s> <s> use ? </s> <s> to get a short listing of all available commands . </s> <s> now what do I do ? </s> <s> well , sit back and enjoy the pouring out of information . </s> <s> if you have something to offer , please feel free to contribute that information to series editor volume editor significant progress has been made recently in shape analysis using neural networks and the energy minimization concept . </s> <s> ablex publishing corporation is planning a special volume on shape analysis , scheduled for this year . </s> <s> this volume will be a part of progress in neural networks , an annual book series reviewing research in modelling , analysis , design and application of neural networks . </s> <s> the primary aim of this volume is to present , in a single volume , the most important achievements made on this important topic , which are otherwise scattered in diverse literature . </s> <s> authors are invited to submit original manuscripts detailing recent progress . </s> <s> suggested topics include , but are not limited to shape modelling , shape estimation , shape recovery , shape representation , shape matching , surface reconstruction and surface decomposition . </s> <s> research work utilizing neural networks directly or based on energy minimization techniques such as markov random field , mean field annealing , simulated annealing , graduated non convexity algorithms and resistive networks are most welcome . </s> <s> plots , bar charts and pie charts . </s> <s> multiple graphs of the same or different sizes may be placed on a single page with multiple lines in each graph . </s> <s> different line styles , widths and colors are supported . </s> <s> a virtually infinite number of distinct area fill patterns may be used . </s> <s> there are almost 1000 characters in the extended character set . </s> <s> this includes four different fonts , the greek alphabet and a host of mathematical , musical , and other symbols . </s> <s> the fonts can be scaled to any size for various effects . </s> <s> many different output device drivers are available system dependent , including a portable metafile format and renderer . </s> <s> freely available but copyrighted via anonymous ftp on hagar.ph.utexas.edu , gle is a high quality graphics package for scientists . </s> <s> it runs on a variety of platforms pcs , vaxes , and unix with drivers for xwindows , regis , tek 4010 , pc graphics cards , vt100s , hp plotters , postscript printers , epson compatible printers and laserjet paintjet printers . </s> <s> it provides latex quality fonts , as well as full support for postscript fonts . </s> <s> the 15 . </s> <s> image analysis software image processing and display pc and mac based tools multi platform software imdisp imdisp written at jpl and other nasa sites . </s> <s> can do simple display , enhancing , smoothing and so on . </s> <s> works with the fits and vicar pds data formats of nasa . </s> <s> can read tiff images , if you know their dimensions pc and macs labview 2 labview is used as a framework for image processing tools . </s> <s> it provides a graphical programming environment using block diagram sketch is the program with graphical elements representing the programming elements . </s> <s> hundreds of functions are already available and are connected using a wiring tool to create the block diagram program . </s> <s> functions that the block diagrams represent include digital signal processing and filtering , numerical analysis , statistics , etc . </s> <s> the tool allows any virtual instrument vi , a software file that looks and acts like a real laboratory instrument to be used as a part of any other virtual instrument . </s> <s> national instruments markets plug in digital signal processing dsp boards for macintoshs and pc compatables that allow real time acquisition and analysis at a personal computer . </s> <s> new software tools for dsp are allowing engineers to harness the power of this technology . </s> <s> the tools range from low level debugging software to high level block diagram development software . </s> <s> there are three levels of dsp programming associated with the nb dsp 2300 board and labview use of the nb dsp 2300 analysis library ffts , power spectra , filters routines callable from think c and macintosh programers workshop mpw c that execute on the nb dsp 2300 board . </s> <s> there is an analysis virtual interface library of ready to use vis optimized for the nb dsp 2300 . </s> <s> use of the national instruments developers toolkit that includes an optimizing c compiler , an assembler and a linker for low level programming of the dsp hardware . </s> <s> this approach offers the highest level of performance but is the must difficult in terms of ease of use . </s> <s> use of the national instruments interface kit software package which has utility functions for memory management data communications and downloading code to the nb dsp 2300 board . </s> <s> this is the easiest route for the development of custom code . </s> <s> ultimage concept vi concept vi by graftek france is a family of image processing virtual instruments vis that give labview 2 described above users high end tools for designing , integrating and monitoring imaging control systems . </s> <s> a vi is a software file that looks and acts like a real laboratory instrument . </s> <s> typical applications for concept vi include thermography , surveillance , machine vision , production testing , biomedical imaging , electronic microscopy and remote sensing . </s> <s> ultimage concept vi addresses applications which require further qualitative and quantitative analysis . </s> <s> it includes a complete set of functions for image enhancement , histogram equalization , spatial and frequency filtering , isolation of features , thresholding , mathematical morphology analysis , density measurement , object counting , sizing and characterization . </s> <s> the program loads images with a minimum resolution of 64 by 64 , a pixel depth of 8 , 16 , or 32 bits , and one image plane . </s> <s> standard input and output formats include pict , tiff , satie , and aipd . </s> <s> other formats can be imported . </s> <s> image enhancement features include lookup table transformations , spatial linear and non linear filters , frequency filtering , arithmetic and logic operations , and geometric transformations , among others . </s> <s> morphological transformations include erosion , dilation , opening , closing , hole removal , object separation , and extraction of skeletons , among others . </s> <s> quantitative analysis provides for objects detection , measurement , and morphological distribution . </s> <s> measures include area , perimeter , center of gravity , moment of inertia , orientation , length of relevant chords , and shape factors and equivalence . </s> <s> measures are saved in ascii format . </s> <s> the program also provides for macro scripting and integration of custom modules . </s> <s> a 3 d view command plots a perspective data graph where image intensity is depicted as mountains or valleys in the plot . </s> <s> the histogram tool can be plotted with either a linear or logarithmic scale . </s> <s> the twenty eight arithmetic and logical operations provide for masking and averaging sections of images , noise removal , making comparisons , etc . </s> <s> there are 13 spatial filters that alter pixel intensities based on local intensity . </s> <s> these include high pass filters for contrast and outlines . </s> <s> the frequency data resulting from fft analysis can be displayed as either the real , imaginary components or the phase , magnitude data . </s> <s> the morphological transformations are useful for data sharpening and defining objects or for removing artifacts . </s> <s> the transformations include thresholding , eroding , dilating and even hole filling . </s> <s> the program s quantitative analysis measurements include area , perimeter , center of mass , object counts , and angle between points . </s> <s> gtfs , inc . </s> <s> 2455 bennett valley road 100c santa rosa , ca 95494 707 579 1733 iplab spectrum iplab spectrum supports image processing and analysis but lacks the morphology and quantitative analysis features provided by graftek franceus ultimage concept vi . </s> <s> using scripting tools , the user tells the system the operations to be performed . </s> <s> the problem is that far too many basic operations require manual intervention . </s> <s> the tool supports ffts , 16 arithmetic operations for pixel alteration , and a movie command for cycling through windows . </s> <s> macintosh based tools ncsa image , ncsa paledit and more ncsa provides a whole suite of public domain visualization tools for the macintosh , 217 355 8925 nih image available at alw.nih.gov 128.231 . </s> <s> 128.7 or preferably zippy.nimh.nih.gov 128.231 . </s> <s> 98.32 , directory pub image . </s> <s> it has painting and image <s> video rate capture , display , processing , and analysis of high resolution monochromatic and color images . </s> <s> includes c source code . </s> <s> tcl image software package for scientific , quantitative image processing and analysis . </s> <s> it provides a complete language for the capture , enhancement , and extraction of quantitative information from gray scale images . </s> <s> feature description disimp incorporates a rich library of image processing utilities and spatial data options . </s> <s> all functions can be easily accessed via the disimp executive . </s> <s> this menu is modular in design and groups image processes by their function . </s> <s> such a logical structure means that complicated processes are simply a progression through a series of modules . </s> <s> processes include image rectification , classification unsupervised and supervised , intensity transformations , three dimensional display and principal component analysis . </s> <s> disimp also supports the more simple and effective enhancement techniques of filtering , band subtraction and ratioing . </s> <s> host configuration requirements running on unix workstations , disimp is capable of processing the more computational intensive techniques in interactive processing times . </s> <s> disimp is available in both runtime and programmer s environments . </s> <s> using the programmers environment , utilities can be developed for specific applications programs . </s> <s> graphics are governed by an icon based display panel which allows quick enhancments of a displayed image . </s> <s> manipulations of look up tables , colour stretches , changes to histograms , zooming and panning can be interactively driven through this control . </s> <s> a range of geographic projections enables disimp to integrate data of image , graphic and textual types . </s> <s> images can be rectified by a number of coordinate systems , providing the true geographic knowledge essential for ground truthing . </s> <s> overlays of grids , text and vector data can be added to further enhance referenced imagery . </s> <s> the system is a flexible package allowing users of various skill levels to determine their own working environment , including the amount of help required . </s> <s> disimp comes fully configured with no optional extras . </s> <s> the purchase price includes all functionality required for professional processing of remote sensed data . </s> <s> for further information , please contact the business manager , clough engineering group systems division , 627 hips human information processing laboratory s image processing system michael landy co wrote and sell a general purpose package for image processing which has been used for basically all the usual image processing applications robotics , medical , satellite , engineering , oil exploration , etc . </s> <s> . </s> <s> it is called hips , and deals with sequences of multiband images in the same way it deals with single images . </s> <s> it has been growing since we first wrote it , both by additions from us as well as a huge user contributed library . </s> <s> feature description hips is a set of image processing modules which together provide a powerful suite of tools for those interested in research , system development and teaching . </s> <s> it handles sequences of images movies in precisely the same manner as single frames . </s> <s> programs and subroutines have been developed for simple image transformations , filtering , convolution , fourier and other transform processing , edge detection and line drawing manipulation , digital image compression and transmission methods , noise generation , and image statistics computation . </s> <s> over 150 such image transformation programs have been developed . </s> <s> as a result , almost any image processing task can be performed quickly and conveniently . </s> <s> additionally , hips allows users to easily integrate their own custom routines . </s> <s> new users become effective using hips on their first day . </s> <s> hips features images that are self documenting . </s> <s> each image stored in the system contains a history of the transformations that have been applied to that image . </s> <s> hips includes a small set of subroutines which primarily deals with a standardized image sequence header , and a large library of image transformation tools in the form of unix filters . </s> <s> it comes complete with source code , on line manual pages , and on line documentation . </s> <s> host configuration requirements originally developed at new york university , hips now represents one of the most extensive and flexible vision and image processing environments currently available . </s> <s> it runs under the unix operating system . </s> <s> it is modular and flexible , provides automatic documentation of its actions , and is almost entirely independent of special equipment . </s> <s> hips is now in use on a variety of computers including vax and microvax , sun , apollo , masscomp , ncr tower , iris , ibm at , etc . </s> <s> for image display and input , drivers are supplied for the grinnell and adage ikonas image processors , and the sun 2 , sun 3 , sun 4 , and sun 386i consoles . </s> <s> we also supply user contributed drivers for a number of other framestores and windowing packages sun gfx , sun console , matrox vip 1024 , iti ip 512 , lexidata , macintosh ii , x windowing system , and iris . </s> <s> the hipsaddon package includes an interface for the crs 4000 . </s> <s> it is a simple matter to interface hips with other frame stores , and we can put interested users in touch with users who have interfaced hips with the arlunya and datacube max video . </s> <s> hips can be easily adapted for other image display devices because 98 of hips is machine independent . </s> <s> availability hips has proven itself a highly flexible system , both as an interactive research tool , and for more production oriented tasks . </s> <s> it is both easy to use , and quickly adapted and extended to new uses . </s> <s> hips is supplied on magnetic tape in unix tar format either reel to reel or sun cartridge , and comes with source code , libraries , a library of convolu tion masks , and on line documentation and manual pages . </s> <s> michael landy sharpimage software p . </s> <s> these are altogether different beasts ! </s> <s> nfotis mira stands for microcomputer image reduction and analysis . </s> <s> mira gives workstation level performance on 386 486 dos computers using svga cards in 256 color modes up to 1024x768 . </s> <s> mira contains a very handsome functional gui which is mouse and keystroke operated . </s> <s> mira reads writes tiff and fits formats , native formats of a number of ccd cameras , and uncompressed binary images in byte , short integer , and 4 byte real pixel format in 1 or 2 dimensions . </s> <s> the result of an image processing operation can be short integer or real pixels , or the same as that of the input image . </s> <s> mira does the operation using short or floating point arithmetic to maintain the precision and accuracy of the pixel format . </s> <s> over 100 functions are hand coded in assembly language for maximum speed on the intel hardware . </s> <s> the entire graphical interface is also written in assembly language to maximize the speed of windowing operations . </s> <s> windows for 2 d image and 1 d image data display and analysis have dedicated cursors which read position and value value in real time as you move the mouse . </s> <s> there are also smooth , real time contrast and brightness stretch and panning of a magnified portion of the displayed image s , all operated by the mouse . </s> <s> a wide selection of grayscale , pseudocolor , and random palettes is provided , and other palettes can be generated . </s> <s> supported functions include such niceties as the following o image image interpolation o image constant o unary operations abs value , polynomial of pixel value , chs , 1 x , log , byteswap , clip values at upper lower limits , short real or real short . </s> <s> o combine directional gradient , line , gaussian , elliptical and rectangular equal weight filters , unsharp masking , median filters , user defined filter kernel . </s> <s> ellipse , rectangle , line , gradient , gaussian , and user defined filters can be rotated to any specified angle . </s> <s> o ccd data reduction flat fielding , dark subtraction , column over underscan bias removal , remove bad pixels and column defects , normalize to region target mean , median , or modal value . </s> <s> o create subimage , mosaic m x n 1 d or 2 d images to get larger image , collapse 2 d image into 1 d image . </s> <s> o plot 1 d section or collapsed section of 2 d image , plot histogram of region of an image . </s> <s> o review change image information header data , rename keywords , plot keyword values for a set of images . </s> <s> o luminance photometry elliptical or circular aperture photometry , brightness profile , isophotal photometry between set of upper lower luminances , area and luminance inside traced polygon . </s> <s> interactive background fitting and removal from part or all of image , fit elliptical aperture shape to image isophotes . </s> <s> o interactive with 2 d point within a polygon in article jonas yngvesson writes intersection between a line and a polygon undecidable ? </s> <s> ? </s> <s> , by dave baraff , tom duff in recent years , many geometric problems have been successfully modeled in a new language called postscript . </s> <s> see postscript language , by adobe systems incorporated , isbn 0 201 1017 9 3 , co . </s> <s> 1985 . </s> <s> so , given a line l and a polygon p , we can write a postscript program that draws the line l and the polygon p , and then outputs the answer . </s> <s> by output , we mean the program executes a command called showpage , which actually prints a page of paper containing the line and the polygon . </s> <s> a quick examination of the paper provides an answer to the reduced problem q , and thus the original problem . </s> <s> curiously , in modern postscript , the point in a polygon problem can be solved even more easily . </s> <s> to wit ! </s> <s> title point in polygon creator allen b for the amusement of comp.graphics regulars languagelevel 2 documentneededresource humor sense thereof endcomments this program will test whether a point is inside a given polygon . </s> <s> currently it uses the even odd rule , but that can be changed by replacing ineofill with infill . </s> <s> these are level 2 operators , so if you ve only got level 1 you re out of luck . </s> <s> the result will be printed on the output stream . </s> <s> caution only accurate to device pixels ! </s> <s> put a huge scale in first if you aren t sure . </s> <s> point to test put x and y coordinates here 50 75 vertices of polygon in counter clockwise order put array of pairs of coordinates here 0 0 100 0 100 100 67 100 67 50 33 50 33 100 0 100 dup 0 get aload pop moveto dup length 1 dup 3 1 roll sub getinterval aload pop lineto forall closepath ineofill yes ! </s> <s> no ! </s> <s> ifelse from chert pellett epson hpgl 4 pen plotter w 340 pens 500 b . </s> <s> o . </s> <s> greetings , I have an  <s> from edward bolson subject re sphere from 4 points ? </s>  <s> I plan to post a summary of responses to this as soon as I have working code , which I will also include . </s>  <s> the intersection of 3 planes method looks best , but my implementation based on a short article in graphics gems I doesn t work . </s>  <s> I may be misinterpreting , of course . </s>  <s> I had avoided the simultaneous solution of the plane equations in favor of dot and cross products , but the former may actually be better . </s>  <s> in either case a matrix determinant needs to be computed implicitly in the solution of linear equations . </s>  <s> to get the planes , I was taking the midpoint of the line from , say , p1 to p2 , and setting the normal as the normalized vector from p1 to p2 . </s>  <s> these just plugged into the formula in graphics gems . </s>  <s> however , the resulting center point is only occasionally equidistant from all 4 of my test points for different tests . </s>  <s> my matrix vector math is very rusty , but it looks like I need to verify the formula , or use the simultaneous equation solution , which will require bringing in another routine I don t have but should be easy to find . </s>  <s> another method is to first find the center of the circle defined by 2 sets of 3 points , and intersecting the normals from there . </s>  <s> this would also define the circle center . </s>  <s> however , small numerical imprecisions would make the lines not intersect . </s>  <s> supposedly 3 planes have to intersect in a unique point if they are not parallel . </s>  <s> ed thanks to all who answered so far . </s>  <s> ed bolson university of washington cardiovascular research 206 543 4535 preferred if you must </s>  <s> from richard mancuso graphics library available via ftp . </s>  <s> I originally wrote the routines as a kind of exercise for myself , but perhaps someone here will find them useful . </s>  <s> they are certainly useable as they are , but are missing some higher level functionality . </s>  <s> they re intended more as an intro to mode 13h programming , a starting point . </s>  <s> the library assumes a 386 processor , but it is trivial to modify it for a 286 . </s>  <s> if enough people ask , I ll make the mods and re post it as a different version . </s>  <s> the routines are written in assembly tasm and are callable from c . </s>  <s> they are fairly simple , but I ve found them to be very fast for my purposes , anyway . </s>  <s> routines are included to enter and exit mode 13h , define a virtual screen , put and get pixels , put a pixmap rectangular image with no transparent spots , put a sprite image with see thru areas , copy areas of the virtual screen into video memory , etc . </s>  <s> I ve also included a simple c routine to draw a line , as well as a c routine to load a 256 color gif image into a buffer . </s>  <s> I also wrote a quick n dirty tm demo program that bounces a bunch of sprites around behind three windows . </s>  <s> the whole package is available on spang.camosun.bc.ca in pub dos vgl.zip it is zipped with pkzip 2.04 g it is completely in the public domain , as far as I m concerned . </s>  <s> do with it whatever you like . </s>  <s> however , it d be nice to get credit where it s due , and maybe an e mail telling me you like it if you don t like it don t bother mark </s>  <s> from arthur stein subject scientific visualization of chemical systems molecules has evolved from an esoteric academic subject into a international industry . </s>  <s> computer graphics has played a decisive role in this transformation by allowing chemists to build , visualize and interact with complex geometrical objects . </s>  <s> while computer scientists are conversant in the language of their own discipline , they are often unfamiliar with the terminology , simulation techniques and practical needs of research chemists . </s>  <s> similarly , chemists are often unfamiliar with the latest paradigms and technological advances in graphical computing . </s>  <s> this interdisciplinary course is intended to bridge the gap between computer science and chemistry and to equip chemistry researchers who wish to be more than just casual users of prepackaged graphics software . </s>  <s> although this is not intended to be a course in computational chemistry or drug design , data sets from chemical research problems will be used in lab and students will be encouraged to bring data sets of their own . </s>  <s> lab exercises and projects will be carried out using data flow programming ibm visualization data explorer software and students will have access to cornell theory center computing resources , including video recording equipment . </s>  <s> audience researchers and students in the chemical and biological sciences interested in integrating state of the art computer graphics into their research computer scientists wishing to gain familiarity with a major application of scientific visualization . </s>  <s> the class size will be limited to 25 participants on a first come first served basis . </s>  <s> level graduate advanced undergraduate , 1 or 2 credits . </s>  <s> may be taken without credit as a workshop . </s>  <s> calculus , linear algebra and introductory chemistry required . </s>  <s> familiarity with unix , x windows and c is useful but not required . </s>  <s> date june 14 25 , 1993 2 credits june 14 18 , 1993 1 or 0 credits time mon fri 9 00 am to 12 00 pm and 1 00 pm to 4 00 pm cost 0 or 1 credit 410 2 credits 820 format the course will be held in the theory center training facility where computer workstations will be available . </s>  <s> daily lectures will be interspersed with laboratory exercises and ample time will be provided for project enablement and familiarization with the new computing environment . </s>  <s> students enrolled for one credit will be graded on the basis of their laboratory exercises and short final project . </s>  <s> those enrolled for a second credit will receive more advanced lectures , be given more time for project development and meet daily to share experience and discuss problems encountered . </s>  <s> content may vary elements of computer graphics polygonal rendering , lighting models , ray tracing , volumetric rendering , stereo graphics , animation , introduction to data flow programming dx , interactivity . </s>  <s> representing the atom size , time and energy scales basic classical and quantum mechanics important categories of molecules small molecules , biopolymers , surfaces and catalysts , miscellaneous current applications data formats and conversions advanced molecular graphics techniques types of simulation and experiment electronic structure , molecular dynamics mechanics electrostatics , x ray crystallography , nmr , quantum dynamics and spectroscopy . </s>  <s> instructors the course will be taught by two instructors . </s>  <s> topics related to computer graphics will be handled by dr . </s>  <s> bruce land , project leader of visualization , cornell national supercomputing facility . </s>  <s> chemistry specific aspects of the course will be handled by dr . </s>  <s> richard e . </s>  <s> gillilan , visualization specialist and research scientist , cornell national supercomputing
