appeared to be very simple and turned out to be quite difficult . </s>  <s> I am wondering if anyone on the net has seen this problem and hopefully some published solutions to it . </s>  <s> the problem is to draw an outline of a surface defined by two roughly parallel cubic splines . </s>  <s> for inputs the problem essentially starts with two sets of points where each set of points is on the edge of an object which we treat as two dimensional , I . </s>  <s> e . </s>  <s> only extant between the edges , but which exists in three dimensional space . </s>  <s> to draw the object we 1 fit a cubic spline through the points . </s>  <s> each spline is effectively computed as a sequence of line segments approximating the curve . </s>  <s> each spline has an equal number of segments . </s>  <s> we assume that the nth segment along each spline is roughly , but not exactly , the same distance along each spline by any reasonable measure . </s>  <s> 2 take each segment n along each spline and match it to the nth segment of the opposing spline . </s>  <s> use the pair of segments to form two triangles which will be filled in to color the surface . </s>  <s> 3 depth sort the triangles 4 take each triangle in sorted order , project onto a 2d pixmap , draw and color the triangle . </s>  <s> take the edge of the triangle that is along the edge of the surface and draw a line along that edge colored with a special edge color it is the edge coloring in step 4 that is at the heart of the problem . </s>  <s> the idea is to effectively outline the edge of the surface . </s>  <s> the net result however generally has lots of breaks and gaps in the edge of the surface . </s>  <s> the reasons for this are fairly complicated . </s>  <s> they involve both rasterization problems and problems resulting from the projecting the splines . </s>  <s> if anything about this problem sounds familiar we would appreciate knowing about other work in this area . </s>  <s> thanks </s>  <s> from robert g . </s>  <s> carpenter subject please recommend 3d graphics library for mac . </s>  <s> hi netters , I m building a cad package and need a 3d graphics library that can handle some writes I am looking for an algorithm to determine if a given point is bound by a polygon . </s>  <s> does anyone have any such code or a reference to book containing information on the subject ? </s>  <s> regards simon basically , there are two algorithms determining whether a point is inside , outside or on the polygon . </s>  <s> the first one is ray or half line method . </s>  <s> in this method , you can draw any ray , if the number of the intersection point of the ray and the polygon is even , then it is outside . </s>  <s> if the number is odd , then it is inside . </s>  <s> of cause , you have to deal with the special cases which may make you headache . </s>  <s> the second method is pi algorithm . </s>  <s> draw the lines between the point and all the vertices on the polygon . </s>  <s> calculate and sum the angles of the successive lines . </s>  <s> if the result is 2 pi , then it is inside . </s>  <s> if pi , then it is on the polygon . </s>  <s> otherwise it is outside . </s>  <s> my experience tells the second method is relible . </s>  <s> hope this helps . </s>  <s> yeh usc </s>  <s> subject re univesa driver from in article , seth wandersman writes I got the univesa using or implementing 3 d interactive applications what types of 3 d widgets you would like to have in your applications . </s>  <s> a 3 d widget is usually located in the same scene as other 3 d objects of the application . </s>  <s> it may let you manipulate application data , the camera , 3 d objects in the scene and so on , or view the status of the application or 3 d objects via the widget s shape , color , position , orientation and so on , or do whatever I missed but you think is possible . </s>  <s> for example , a manipulative widget can be virtual trackball shown as a partially transparent sphere super imposed on the object to be rotated . </s>  <s> a feedback widget can be a ruler with ends anchored to 2 objects . </s>  <s> the length of the ruler changes as the objects move and a numeric value is shown on the ruler indicating the distance . </s>  <s> a widget can provide both manipulation and feedback . </s>  <s> for example , the ruler can be used to change the distance between the objects along its own axis . </s>  <s> please e mail me or post your opinions on 3 d interaction . </s>  <s> the information I gathered will help me design a 3 d ui construction tool . </s>  <s> your help is very much appreciated . </s>  <s> tony lau m.sc . </s>  <s> student dept . </s>  <s> of computer science </s>  <s> from ederveen d . </s>  <s> subject micro arrange a trip to the annual conference could reduce this to 27 by selecting siggraph lite , which means siggraph is charging an additional 32 or so for the proceedings and the art show catalog , essentially . </s>  <s> toplas went up 40 in cost , way outstripping the current inflation rate . </s>  <s> basic sigchi fees remainded the same , but whereas before sigchi membership included uist and human factors conferences proceedings , these are now an extra cost option . </s>  <s> bundling that back into the basic rate , equivalent services have gone up 100 in cost . </s>  <s> sigois membership cost has up 33 , but they ve also split out the computer supported cooperative work conference proceedings that used to be included with membership . </s>  <s> adding that cost back in means this sig also has doubled its membership fee . </s>  <s> what really galls me is that the acm sent out brochures a couple months ago touting their new approach to providing member services , and tried to make it sound like they were offering new services . </s>  <s> but with the exception of a couple , like siggraph , all the plus services appear to be just splitting the costs into smaller piles so that they don t look so big . </s>  <s> but their recommended changes to my membership would have me paying 90 more than last year for a 31 increase in services measured by cost , not by routine . </s>  <s> I ve tried a couple without much luck . </s>  <s> please e mail responses and I will post a summary of any replies . </s>  <s> thank you . </s>  <s> richard stoakley the problem is not precisely defined above , but if you need to find the smallest convex polygon that encloses a given polygon , then you are seeking the convex hull of your original polygon . </s>  <s> there are two ways to do this use a somewhat tricky but by now well examined linear time algorithm that exploits the polygon boundary , or just feed the vertices of the original polygon to a convex hull routine and accept o n log n . </s>  <s> both methods are discussed in preparata and shamos , for example . </s>  <s> from wayne rigby subject re need gif iff file format in article 1rkjm5 ramin taraz writes could somebody please email me some info on either what gif or iff file formats are , or where I can get such info ? </s>  <s> well , gif stands for graphics interchange format and was put forth by compuserve back in 1987 ? </s>  <s> or so . </s>  <s> it was to create a format that could be read and displayed by any system . </s>  <s> gif is limited to 8 bit color but has a built in compression scheme lzw ? </s>  <s> . </s>  <s> iff is not really a graphics format , but rather a standard way to package images , sounds , animations , text , or whatever into one file . </s>  <s> iff was created by electronic arts , I do believe I could be wrong , for the amiga . </s>  <s> it was quickly adopted as pretty much the standard file format for the amiga . </s>  <s> the most common image format for the iff package is an ilbm interleaved bitmap ? </s>  <s> but many others exist . </s>  <s> this format supports 24 bit color images . </s>  <s> information on both of these and many more are available via anonymous ftp at zamenhof.cs.rice.edu in the directory pub graphics.formats taken from the faq for this news group . </s>  <s> wayne rigby </s>  <s> from kevin martin subject re tiff  <s> the clock rate is 14,7 mhz when loading an image with 512 pixel in the line and 7,4 mhz when loading a 256 pixels image . </s>  <s> this provides the equal pixel size of input image in both horizontal and vertical directions . </s>  <s> the number of gray levels in any input modes is 256 . </s>  <s> video signal capture time 2.5 s . </s>  <s> controller vs52 the purpose of the controller is to enter the tv images into a ibm pc at or any other machine of that type . </s>  <s> the controller was created on the base of modern elements , including user programmable gate arrays . </s>  <s> the controller allows to digitize a input signal with different resolutions . </s>  <s> its flexible architecture makes possible to change technical parameters . </s>  <s> instead of tv signal one can process any other analog signal including signals from slow speed scanning devices . </s>  <s> the controller has the following technical characteristics memory volume from 256 k to 2 mb resolution when working with standard video signal from 64x64 to 1024x512 pixels resolution when working in slow input regime up to 2048x1024 pixels video signal capture time 40 ms . </s>  <s> maximum size of a screen when memory volume is 2mb 2048x1024 pixels number of gray level 256 clock rate for input up to 30 mhz 4 input video multiplexer input output lookup table lut possibility to realize scroll and zoom 8 lines for external synchronization an input using external controlling signal electronic adjustment of black and white reference for analog digital converter possibility output image to the color rgb monitor . </s>  <s> one can change all listed above functions and parameters of the controller by reprogramming it . </s>  <s> image processor vs100 image processor vs100 allows to digitize and process tv signal in real time . </s>  <s> it is possible digitize tv signal with 512 512 8 resolution and realize arithmetic and logic operation with two images . </s>  <s> processor was created on the base of modern elements including user programmable gate arrays and designed as a board for pc . </s>  <s> memory volume allows write to the 256 frames with 512 512 8 format . </s>  <s> it is possible to accumulate until 16 images . </s>  <s> the processor has the following technical characteristics memory volume to 64 mb number of the gray level 256 4 input video multiplexer input output lookup table electronic adjustment for black and white adc reference image size from 256 256 to 8192 8192 possibility color and black white output possibility input from slow scan video sources . </s> re fast polygon routine needed lucas adamski writes in article ian d romanick writes what kind of polygons ? </s>  <s> shaded ? </s>  <s> texturemapped ? </s>  <s> hm ? </s>  <s> more comes into play with fast routines than just polygons . </s>  <s> it would be nice to know exaclty what system vga is a start , but what processor ? </s>  <s> and a few of the specifics of the implementation . </s>  <s> you need to give more info if you want to get any answers ! </s>  <s> p I don t want texture mapped , cause if I did I d asked for them . </s>  <s> just a simple and fast routine to do filled polygons . </s>  <s> as for the processor , it d be for a minimum of a 286 ... maybe 386 if I can t find a good one for 286s . </s>  <s> ideally , I want a polyn function that can clip to a user defined viewport , and write to an arbitrary location in memory . </s>  <s> of course the chances of ok it is for a game that is 3d and you have listed the characteristics that you are looking for . </s>  <s> I think you may have left out a few important parameters . </s>  <s> the polygons are all convex . </s>  <s> they have less than n sides . </s>  <s> you are drawing meshes walls doors etc . </s>  <s> I believe that the algorithms you can get that will only draw convex polygons can be much more efficient than those that can draw concave self intersecting polygons . </s>  <s> this efficiency can largely be attributed to the fact that simple convex polygons only have a left and a right edge on each scan line . </s>  <s> complex figure 8 type polygons can be a bit trickier . </s>  <s> the less than n sides specification especially if it is a very small number like 3 or 4 allow othe optimisations to be made . </s>  <s> thus for a high speed game application I think you are looking for code that exploits and is hence limited to drawing simple convex polygons . </s>  <s> finding something like that are pretty remote , so I guess I d need the source with it . </s>  <s> oh , and I guess it would need to be in asm otherwise it d be too slow . </s>  <s> I ve seen some polygon routines in c , and they ve all been waaay too slow . </s>  <s> its for a 3d vector graphics program . </s>  <s> I ve been hunting high and low it may have been that they were very general purpose algorithms . </s>  <s> if you limit yourself to 3 or four sided simple convex polygons I think data systems phone 313 696 6302 note the views and opinions expressed herein are mine , and do not reflect those of electronic data systems corp . </s>  <s> from robert grant subject virtual reality for x on the cheap ! </s>  <s> hi everyone , I thought that some people may be interested in my vr software on these groups announcing the release of multiverse 1.0 . </s>  <s> 2 multiverse is a multi user , non immersive , x windows based virtual reality system , primarily focused on entertainment research . </s>  <s> features client server based model , using berkeley sockets . </s>  <s> no limit to the number of users apart from performance . </s>  <s> generic clients . </s>  <s> customizable servers . </s>  <s> hierachical objects allowing attachment of cameras and light sources . </s>  <s> multiple light sources ambient , point and spot . </s>  <s> objects can have extension code , to handle unique functionality , easily attached . </s>  <s> functionality client the client is built around a fast render loop . </s>  <s> basically it changes things when told to by the server and then renders an image from the user s viewpoint . </s>  <s> it also provides the server with information about the user s actions which can then be communicated to other clients and therefore to other users . </s>  <s> the client is designed to be generic in other words you don t need to develop a new client when you want to enter a new world . </s>  <s> this means that resources can be spent on enhancing the client software rather than adapting it . </s>  <s> the adaptations , as will be explained in a moment , occur in the servers . </s>  <s> this release of the client software supports the following functionality o hierarchical objects with associated addressing o multiple light sources and types ambient , point and spot o user interface panels o colour polygonal rendering with phong shading optional wireframe for faster frame rates o mouse and keyboard input some people may be disappointed that this software doesn t support the powerglove as an input device this is not because it can t , but because I don t have one ! </s>  <s> this will , however , be one of the first enhancements ! </s>  <s> server s this is where customization can take place . </s>  <s> the following basic support is provided in this release for potential world server developers o transparent client management o client message handling this may not sound like much , but it takes away the headache of accepting and terminating clients and receiving messages from them the application writer can work with the assumption that things are happening locally . </s>  <s> things get more interesting in the object extension functionality . </s>  <s> this is what is provided to allow you to animate your objects o server selectable extension installation what this means is that you can decide which objects have extended functionality in your world . </s>  <s> basically you call the extension initialisers you want . </s>  <s> o event handler registration when you develop extensions for an object you basically write callback functions for the events that you want the object to respond to . </s>  <s> current events supported init , move , change , collide terminate o collision detection registration if you want your object to respond to collision events just provide some basic information to the collision detection management software . </s>  <s> your callback will be activated when a collision occurs . </s>  <s> this software is kept separate from the worldserver applications because the application developer wants to build a library of extended objects from which to choose . </s>  <s> the following is all you need to make a world server application o provide an initworld function this is where you choose what object extensions will be supported , plus any initialization you want to do . </s>  <s> o provide a positionobject function this is where you determine where to place a new client . </s>  <s> o provide an installworldobjects function this is where you load the world . </s>  <s> wld file for a new client . </s>  <s> o provide a getworldtype function this is where you tell a new client what persona they should have . </s>  <s> o provide an animateworld function this is where you can go wild ! </s>  <s> at a minimum you should let the objects move by calling a move function and let the server sleep for a bit to avoid outrunning the clients . </s>  <s> that s all there is to it ! </s>  <s> and to prove it here are the line counts for the three world servers I ve provided generic 81 lines dactyl 270 lines more complicated collision detection due to the stairs ! </s>  <s> will probably be improved with future versions dogfight 72 lines location this software is located at the following site ftp.u.washington.edu directory pub virtual worlds file multiverse 1.0.2.tar . </s>  <s> z futures client o texture mapping . </s>  <s> o more realistic rendering I . </s>  <s> e . </s>  <s> z buffering or similar , gouraud shading o hmd support . </s>  <s> o etc , etc ... server o physical modelling gravity , friction etc . </s>  <s> o enhanced object management interaction o etc , etc ... both o improved comms ! </s>  <s> ! </s>  <s> ! </s>  <s> I hope this provides people with a good understanding of the multiverse software , unfortunately it comes with practically zero documentation , and I m not sure whether that will ever be able to be rectified ! </s>  <s> I hope people enjoy this software and that it is useful in our explorations of the virtual universe I ve certainly found fascinating developing it , and I would love to add support for the powerglove ... and an hmd ! </s>  <s> ! </s>  <s> finally one major disclaimer this is totally amateur code . </s>  <s> by that I mean there is no support for this code other than what I , out the kindness of my heart , or you , out of pure desperation , provide . </s>  <s> I cannot be held responsible for anything good or bad that may happen through the use of this code use it at your own risk ! </s>  <s> disclaimer over ! </s>  <s> of course if you love it , I would like to here from you . </s>  <s> and anyone with positive contributions criticisms is also encouraged to contact me . </s>  <s> anyone who hates it dev null ! </s> from frederic leymarie subject re developable surface in article , abel writes hi netters , I am currently doing some investigations on developable surface . </s>  <s> can anyone familiar with this </s>  <s> you can lay it or roll it flat on the plane it may require you to give it a cut though ... e . </s>  <s> g . </s>  <s> , a cylinder , a cone , a plane of course ! </s>  <s> or any surface or patch having vanishing gaussian intrinsic curvature I . </s>  <s> e . </s>  <s> , with singular hessian , the matrix of 2nd derivatives for an adequate coordinate patch are developable . </s>  <s> in more technical words , a developable surface is locally isometric to a plane at all points . </s>  <s> think also of the sphere or the earth which in a non developable whatever way s you cut it , you will not be able to lay flat any pieces of it ... its intrinsic curvature is nowhere vanishing . </s>  <s> for more details on this look at any book on differential geometry which treats surfaces 2d manifolds e . </s>  <s> g . </s>  <s> , m . </s>  <s> do carmo s book book carmo 76differential , author do carmo , manfredo p . </s>  <s> , title differential geometry of curves and surfaces , year stefan eckart subject dmpeg10.zip info another dos mpeg decoder player posted I have posted a dos mpeg decoder player to alt.binaries.pictures.utilities . </s>  <s> here is a short description and some technical information , taken from the accompanying documentation dmpeg v1 . </s>  <s> 0 public domain mpeg decoder by stefan eckart 0 . </s>  <s> features dmpeg dmplay is another mpeg decoder player for the pc decodes nearly the full mpeg video standard I , p , b frames , frame size up to at least 352x240 supported saves decoded sequence in 8 or 24bit raw file for later display optional on screen display during decoding requires vga several dithering options ordered dither , floyd steinberg , grayscale color space selection runs under dos , 640kb ram , no ms windows required very compact small code small data models , 16 bit arithmetic real time display of the raw file by a separate player for vga and many super vgas ... 4 . </s>  <s> technical information the player is a rather straightforward implementation of the mpeg spec 1 . </s>  <s> the idct is based on the chen wang 13 multiplication algorithm 2 not quite the optimum , I know . </s>  <s> blocks with not more than eight non zero coefficients use a non separated direct multiply accumulate 2d idct sounds great , doesn t it ? </s>  <s> , which turned out to be faster than a fast algorithm in this quite common case . </s>  <s> dithering is pretty standard . </s>  <s> main difference to the berkeley decoder except for the fewer number of supported algorithms is the use of 256 instead of 128 colors , the default option to use a restricted color space and the implementation of a color saturation dominant ordered dither . </s>  <s> this leads to a significantly superior quality of the dithered image I claim , judge yourself . </s>  <s> restricted color space means that the u and v components are clipped to 0.25 instead of 0.5 and the display color space points are distributed over this restricted space . </s>  <s> since the distance between color space points is thus reduced by a factor of two , the color resolution is doubled at the expense of not being able to represent fully saturated colors . </s>  <s> saturation dominant ordered dither is a method by which a color , lying somewhere between the points of the display color space , is approximated by primarily alternating between two points of constant hue instead of constant saturation . </s>  <s> this yields subjectivly better quality due to the lower sensitivity of the human viewing system to saturation changes than to hue changes the same reasoning as used by the pal tv standard to improve on ntsc . </s>  <s> the improvement is particularly visible in dark brown or redish areas . </s>  <s> ... stefan eckart , </s>  <s> directly to internet mail to thanks </s>  <s> from kenneth sloan subject re removing distortion from bitmapped drawings ? </s>  <s> in article earl boebert writes let s say you have a scanned image of a line drawing in this case a boat , but it could be anything . </s>  <s> on the drawing you have a set of reference points whose true x , y positions are known . </s>  <s> now you digitize the drawing manually in this case , using yaron danon s excellent digitize program . </s>  <s> that is , you use a program which converts cursor positions to x , y and saves those values when you click the mouse . </s>  <s> upon digitizing you notice that the reference point values that come out of the digitizing process differ in small but significant ways from the known true values . </s>  <s> this is understandable because the scanned drawing is a reproduction of the original and there are successive sources of distortion such as differential expansion and contraction of paper , errors introduced in the printing process , scanner errors and what have you . </s>  <s> the errors are not uniform over the entire drawing , so global adjustments such as stretching contracting uniformly over x or y , or rotating the whole drawing , are not satisfactory . </s>  <s> so the question is does any kind soul know of an algorithm for removing such distortion ? </s>  <s> in particular , if I have three sets of points reference x , y the known true values distortedreference x , y the same points , with known errors distorteddata x , y other points , with unknown errors what function of reference and distorted could I apply to distorteddata to remove the errors . </s>  <s> I suspect the problem could be solved by treating the distorted reference points as resulting from the projection of a bumpy 3d surface , solving for the surface and then flattening it to remove the errors in the other data points . </s>  <s> it helps to have some idea of the source of the distortion or at least a reasonable model of the class of distortion . </s>  <s> below is a very short description of the process which we use if you have further questions , feel free to poke me via e mail . </s>  <s> assume locally smooth distortion 0 compute the delaunay triangulation of your x , y points . </s>  <s> this defines the set of neighbors for each point . </s>  <s> if your data are not naturally convex , you may have very long edges on the convex hull . </s>  <s> consider deleting these edges . </s>  <s> 1 now , there are two goals a move the distorteddata x , y to the reference x , y b keep the length e as measured from the current x , y s as close as possible to the digitizedlength e as measured using the digitized x , y s . </s>  <s> 2 for every point , compute a displacement based on a and b . </s>  <s> for example a for x , y points for which you know the reference x , y , you can move alpha 0 reference x , y current x , y . </s>  <s> this will slowly move the distortedreference x , y towards the reference x , y . </s>  <s> b for all other points , examine the current length of each edge . </s>  <s> for each edge , compute a displacement which would make that edge the correct length where correct is the digitizedlength . </s>  <s> take the vector sum of these edge displacements , and move the point alpha 1 sumofedgedisplacements . </s>  <s> this will keep the triangulated mesh consistent with your digitized mesh . </s>  <s> 3 iterate 2 until you are happy for example , no point moves very much . </s>  <s> alpha 0 and alpha 1 need to be determined by experimentation . </s>  <s> consider how much you believe the reference x , y I . </s>  <s> e . </s>  <s> , do you absolutely insist on the final points exactly matching the references , or do you want to balance some error in matching the reference against changes in length of the edges . </s>  <s> warning there are a couple of geometric invariants which must be observed essentially , you can t allow the convex hull to change , and you can t allow triangles to fold over neighboring triangles . </s>  <s> both of these can be handled either by special case checks on the motion of individual points , or by periodically re triangulating the points using the current positions but still calculating digitizedlength from the original positions . </s>  <s> when we first did this , the triangulation time was prohibitive , so we only did it once . </s>  <s> if I were motivated to try and change code that has been working in production mode for 5 years , I might go back and re triangulate on every iteration . </s>  <s> if you have more compute power than you know what to do with , you might consider having every point interact with every other point ... but first read up on linear solutions to the n body problem . </s>  <s> there are lots of papers in the last 10 years of siggraph proceedings on springs , constraints , and energy calculations which are relevant . </s>  <s> the above method is described , in more or less detail in inproceedings sloan 86 , author sloan , jr . </s>  <s> , kenneth r . </s>  <s> and david meyers and christine a . </s>  <s> curcio , title reconstruction and display of the retina , booktitle proceedings graphics interface 86 vision interface 86 , address vancouver , canada , pages 385 389 , month may , year 1986 techreport curcio 87b , author christine a . </s>  <s> curcio and kenneth r . </s>  <s> sloan and david meyers , title computer methods for sampling , reconstruction , display , and analysis of retinal whole mounts , number tr 87 12 03 , institution department of computer science , university of washington , address seattle , wa , month december , year 1987 article curcio 89 , author christine a . </s>  <s> curcio and kenneth r . </s>  <s> sloan and david meyers , title computer methods for sampling , reconstruction , display , and analysis of retinal whole mounts , journal vision research , volume 29 , number 5 , pages 529 540 , year 1989 kenneth sloan computer and information sciences university of alabama at birmingham 205 934 2213 115a campbell hall , uab station 205 934 5473 fax birmingham , al 35294 1170 and will play in the same amount of time on any machine . </s>  <s> however , an lc will drop frames in order to keep the sound and video synced up . </s>  <s> the centris and quadras have similar <s> thanks </s>  <s> from lawrence d oliveiro , waikato university subject quicktime performance was re rumours about 3do ? </s>  <s> ? </s>  <s> ? </s>  <s> ok , with all the discussion about observed playback speeds with quicktime , the effects of scaling and so on , I thought I d do some more tests . </s>  <s> first of all , I felt that my original speed test was perhaps less than realistic . </s>  <s> the movie I had been using only had 18 frames in it it was a version of the very first movie I created with the compact video compressor . </s>  <s> I decided something a little longer would give closer to real world results for better or for worse . </s>  <s> I pulled out a copy of 2001 a space odyssey that I had recorded off tv a while back . </s>  <s> about fifteen minutes into the movie , there s a sequence where the earth shuttle is approaching the space station . </s>  <s> specifically , I digitized a portion of about 30 seconds duration , zooming in on the rotating space station . </s>  <s> I figured this would give a reasonable amount of movement between frames . </s>  <s> to increase the differences between frames , I digitized it at only 5 frames per second , to give a total of 171 frames . </s>  <s> I captured the raw footage at a resolution of 384 288 pixels with the spigot card in my centris 650 quarter size resolution from a pal source . </s>  <s> I then imported it into premiere and put it through the compact video compressor , keeping the 5 fps frame rate . </s>  <s> I created two versions of the movie one scaled to 320 240 resolution , the other at 160 120 resolution . </s>  <s> I used the default 2.00 quality setting in premiere 2.0 . </s>  <s> 1 , and specified a key frame every ten frames . </s>  <s> I then ran the 320 240 movie through the same raw speed test program I used for the results I d been reporting earlier . </s>  <s> result a playback rate of over 45 frames per second . </s>  <s> that s right , I was getting a much higher result than with that first short test movie . </s>  <s> just for fun , I copied the 320 240 movie to my external hard disk a quantum lp105s , and ran it from there . </s>  <s> this time the playback rate was only about 35 frames per second . </s>  <s> obviously the 230mb internal hard disk also a quantum is a significant contributor to the speed of playback . </s>  <s> I modified my speed test program to allow the specification of optional scaling factors , and tried playing back the 160 120 movie scaled to 320 240 size . </s>  <s> this time the playback speed was over 60 fps . </s>  <s> clearly , the poster who observed poor performance on scaled playback was seeing quicktime 1.0 in action , not 1.5 . </s>  <s> I d try my tests with quicktime 1.0 , but I don t think it s entirely compatible with my centris and system 7.1 ... unscaled , the playback rate for the 160 120 movie was over 100 fps . </s>  <s> the other thing I tried was saving versions of the 320 240 movie with preferred playback rates greater than 1.0 , and seeing how well they played from within movieplayer ie with quicktime s normal synchronized playback . </s>  <s> a preferred rate of 9.0 45 fps didn t work too well the playback was very jerky . </s>  <s> compare this with the raw speed test , which achieved 45 fps with ease . </s>  <s> I can t believe that quicktime s synchronization code would add this much overhead I think the slowdown was coming from the mac system s task switching . </s>  <s> a preferred rate of 7.0 35 fps seemed to work fine I couldn t see any evidence of stutter . </s>  <s> at 8.0 40 fps I think I could see slight stutter , but with four key frames every second , it was hard to tell . </s>  <s> I guess I could try recreating the movies with a longer interval between the key frames , to make the stutter more noticeable . </s>  <s> of course , this will also improve the compression slightly , which should speed up the playback performance even more ... lawrence d oliveiro fone 64 7 856 2889 computer services dept fax 64 7 838 4066 university of waikato electric mail hamilton , new zealand 37 47 26 s , 175 19 7 e , gmt 12 00 </s>  <s> from subject system cpu hd array framebuffer which can play and record hdtv quality moving picture in realtime . </s>  <s> hdtv has about 6mb frame , so recording playing moving picture will need about 180mb sec bandwidth . </s>  <s> I m thinking to treat the raw data .. not compressed . </s>  <s> actually , for digital hdtv systems that s far higher bandwidth than you need , unless there s some reason you must work in fully uncompressed hdtv . </s>  <s> also , my calculations is that each frame should be well under 6mb , even using 24 bits pixel which is more bits than you actually need 15 or 18 should be enough for a moving picture . </s>  <s> 1600x1100x16bits is 3.5 mb I m guessing at hdtv resolution it may be a bit wider than 1600 , I m fairly sure of the 1100 number for most of the digital proposals . </s>  <s> I hope you have a very fast memory system as well 180mb s while displaying will require a heavily interleaved vram system . </s>  <s> unless you have a very compelling reason , I d advise trying to use at least somewhat compressed data . </s>  <s> you don t have to go to full compression to get to a level where the data io requirements are much cheaper and easier to deal with subject sphere from 4 points another method is to first find the center of the circle defined by 2 sets of 3 points , and intersecting the normals from there . </s>  <s> this would also define the circle center . </s>  <s> however , small numerical imprecisions would make the lines not intersect . </s>  <s> supposedly 3 planes have to intersect in a unique point if they are not parallel . </s>  <s> having thought about this , why don t you project the 2 lines onto the 2d plane formed by the lines . </s>  <s> do an intersection calculation in the plane in 2d , where you re guaranteed a unique solution unless they re parallel which won t happen in this case , and then use parametric distance along the lines from the circle centres to determine the exact point of interest . </s>  <s> this bypasses the messy error propogation required to do the calculation in 3d . </s>  <s> hope I haven t put my foot in it again ! </s>  <s> steve steven collins email visiting computer graphics cs.cmu.edu tom lane subject jpeg image compression frequently asked questions archive name jpeg faq last modified 16 may 1993 this faq article discusses jpeg image compression . </s>  <s> suggestions for additions and clarifications are welcome . </s>  <s> new since version of 2 may 1993 added info on imageviewer for next . </s>  <s> this article includes the following sections 1 what is jpeg ? </s>  <s> 2 why use jpeg ? </s>  <s> 3 when should I use jpeg , and when should I stick with gif ? </s>  <s> 4 how well does jpeg compress images ? </s>  <s> 5 what are good quality settings for jpeg ? </s>  <s> 6 where can I get jpeg software ? </s>  <s> 6a canned software , viewers , etc . </s>  <s> 6b source code 7 what s all this hoopla about color quantization ? </s>  <s> 8 how does jpeg work ? </s>  <s> 9 what about lossless jpeg ? </s>  <s> 10 why all the argument about file formats ? </s>  <s> 11 how do I recognize which file format I have , and what do I do about it ? </s>  <s> 12 what about arithmetic coding ? </s>  <s> 13 does loss accumulate with repeated compression decompression ? </s>  <s> 14 what are some rules of thumb for converting gif images to jpeg ? </s>  <s> sections 1 6 are basic info that every jpeg user needs to know sections 7 14 are advanced info for the curious . </s>  <s> this article is posted every 2 weeks . </s>  <s> you can always find the latest version in the news.answers archive at rtfm.mit.edu 18.70 . </s>  <s> 0.226 . </s>  <s> by ftp , fetch pub usenet news.answers jpeg faq or if you don t have ftp , send e mail to with body send usenet news.answers jpeg faq . </s>  <s> many other faq articles are also stored in this archive . </s>  <s> for more instructions on use of the archive , send e mail to the same address with the words help and index no quotes on separate lines . </s>  <s> if you don t get a reply , the server may be misreading your return address add a line such as path myname mysite to specify your correct e mail address to reply to . </s>  <s> 1 what is jpeg ? </s>  <s> jpeg pronounced jay peg is a standardized image compression mechanism . </s>  <s> jpeg stands for joint photographic experts group , the original name of the committee that wrote the standard . </s>  <s> jpeg is designed for compressing either full color or gray scale digital images of natural , real world scenes . </s>  <s> it does not work so well on non realistic images , such as cartoons or line drawings . </s>  <s> jpeg does not handle black and white 1 bit per pixel images , nor does it handle motion picture compression . </s>  <s> standards for compressing those types of images are being worked on by other committees , named jbig and mpeg respectively . </s>  <s> jpeg is lossy , meaning that the image you get out of decompression isn t quite identical to what you originally put in . </s>  <s> the algorithm achieves much of its compression by exploiting known limitations of the human eye , notably the fact that small color details aren t perceived as well as small details of light and dark . </s>  <s> thus , jpeg is intended for compressing images that will be looked at by humans . </s>  <s> if you plan to machine analyze your images , the small errors introduced by jpeg may be a problem for you , even if they are invisible to the eye . </s>  <s> a useful property of jpeg is that the degree of lossiness can be varied by adjusting compression parameters . </s>  <s> this means that the image maker can trade off file size against output image quality . </s>  <s> you can make extremely small files if you don t mind poor quality this is useful for indexing image archives , making thumbnail views or icons , etc . </s>  <s> etc . </s>  <s> conversely , if you aren t happy with the output quality at the default compression setting , you can jack up the quality until you are satisfied , and accept lesser compression . </s>  <s> 2 why use jpeg ? </s>  <s> there are two good reasons to make your image files smaller , and to store 24 bit per pixel color data instead of 8 bit per pixel data . </s>  <s> making image files smaller is a big win for transmitting files across networks and for archiving libraries of images . </s>  <s> being able to compress a 2 mbyte full color file down to 100 kbytes or so makes a big difference in disk space and transmission time ! </s>  <s> if you are comparing gif and jpeg , the size ratio is more like four to one . </s>  <s> more details below . </s>  <s> if your viewing software doesn t support jpeg directly , you ll have to convert jpeg to some other format for viewing or manipulating images . </s>  <s> even with a jpeg capable viewer , it takes longer to decode and view a jpeg image than to view an image of a simpler format gif , for instance . </s>  <s> thus , using jpeg is essentially a time space tradeoff you give up some time in order to store or transmit an image more cheaply . </s>  <s> it s worth noting that when network or phone transmission is involved , the time savings from transferring a shorter file can be much greater than the extra time to decompress the file . </s>  <s> I ll let you do the arithmetic yourself . </s>  <s> the other reason why jpeg will gradually replace gif as a standard usenet posting format is that jpeg can store full color information 24 bits pixel 16 million colors instead of 8 or less 256 or fewer colors . </s>  <s> if you have only 8 bit display hardware then this may not seem like much of an advantage to you . </s>  <s> within a couple of years , though , 8 bit gif will look as obsolete as black and white macpaint format does today . </s>  <s> furthermore , for reasons detailed in section 7 , jpeg is far more useful than gif for exchanging images among people with widely varying color display hardware . </s>  <s> hence jpeg is considerably more appropriate than gif for use as a usenet posting standard . </s>  <s> 3 when should I use jpeg , and when should I stick with gif ? </s>  <s> jpeg is not going to displace gif entirely for some types of images , gif is superior in image quality , file size , or both . </s>  <s> one of the first things to learn about jpeg is which kinds of images to apply it to . </s>  <s> as a rule of thumb , jpeg is superior to gif for storing full color or gray scale images of realistic scenes that means scanned photographs and similar material . </s>  <s> jpeg is superior even if you don t have 24 bit display hardware , and it is a lot superior if you do . </s>  <s> see section 7 for details . </s>  <s> gif does significantly better on images with only a few distinct colors , such as cartoons and line drawings . </s>  <s> in particular , large areas of pixels that are all exactly the same color are compressed very efficiently indeed by gif . </s>  <s> jpeg can t squeeze these files as much as gif does without introducing visible defects . </s>  <s> this sort of image is best kept in gif form . </s>  <s> in particular , single color borders are quite cheap in gif files , but they should be avoided in jpeg files . </s>  <s> jpeg also has a hard time with very sharp edges a row of pure black pixels adjacent to a row of pure white pixels , for example . </s>  <s> sharp edges tend to come out blurred unless you use a very high quality setting . </s>  <s> again , this sort of thing is not found in scanned photographs , but it shows up fairly often in gif files borders , overlaid text , etc . </s>  <s> the blurriness is particularly objectionable with text that s only a few pixels high . </s>  <s> if you have a gif with a lot of small size overlaid text , don t jpeg it . </s>  <s> computer drawn images ray traced scenes , for instance usually fall between scanned images and cartoons in terms of complexity . </s>  <s> the more complex and subtly rendered the image , the more likely that jpeg will do well on it . </s>  <s> the same goes for semi realistic artwork fantasy drawings and such . </s>  <s> plain black and white two level images should never be converted to jpeg . </s>  <s> you need at least about 16 gray levels before jpeg is useful for gray scale images . </s>  <s> it should also be noted that gif is lossless for gray scale images of up to 256 levels , while jpeg is not . </s>  <s> if you have an existing library of gif images , you may wonder whether you should convert them to jpeg . </s>  <s> you will lose a little image quality if you do . </s>  <s> section 7 , which argues that jpeg image quality is superior to gif , only applies if both formats start from a full color original . </s>  <s> if you start from a gif , you ve already irretrievably lost a great deal of information jpeg can only make things worse . </s>  <s> however , the disk space savings may justify converting anyway . </s>  <s> this is a decision you ll have to make for yourself . </s>  <s> if you do convert a gif library to jpeg , see section 14 for hints . </s>  <s> be prepared to leave some images in gif format , since some gifs will not convert well . </s>  <s> 4 how well does jpeg compress images ? </s>  <s> pretty darn well . </s>  <s> here are some sample file sizes for an image I have handy , a 727x525 full color image of a ship in a harbor . </s>  <s> the first three files are for comparison purposes the rest were created with the free jpeg software described in section 6b . </s>  <s> file size in bytes comments ship.ppm 1145040 original file in ppm format no compression 24 bits or 3 bytes per pixel , plus a few bytes overhead ship.ppm . </s>  <s> z 963829 ppm file passed through unix compress compress doesn t accomplish a lot , you ll note . </s>  <s> other text oriented compressors give similar results . </s>  <s> ship.gif 240438 converted to gif with ppmquant fs 256 ppmtogif most of the savings is the result of losing color info gif saves 8 bits pixel , not 24 . </s>  <s> see sec . </s>  <s> 7 . </s>  <s> ship . </s>  <s> jpg 95 155622 cjpeg q 95 highest useful quality setting this is indistinguishable from the 24 bit original , at least to my nonprofessional eyeballs . </s>  <s> ship . </s>  <s> jpg 75 58009 cjpeg q 75 default setting you have to look mighty darn close to distinguish this from the original , even with both on screen at once . </s>  <s> ship . </s>  <s> jpg 50 38406 cjpeg q 50 this has slight defects if you know what to look for , you could tell it s been jpeged without seeing the original . </s>  <s> still as good image quality as many recent postings in usenet pictures groups . </s>  <s> ship . </s>  <s> jpg 25 25192 cjpeg q 25 jpeg s characteristic blockiness becomes apparent at this setting djpeg blocksmooth helps some . </s>  <s> still , I ve seen plenty of usenet postings that were of poorer image quality than this . </s>  <s> ship . </s>  <s> jpg 5o 6587 cjpeg q 5 optimize optimize cuts table overhead blocky , but perfectly satisfactory for preview or indexing purposes . </s>  <s> note that this file is tiny the compression ratio from the original is 173 1 ! </s>  <s> in this case jpeg can make a file that s a factor of four or five smaller than a gif of comparable quality the q 75 file is every bit as good as the gif , better if you have a full color display . </s>  <s> this seems to be a typical ratio for real world scenes . </s>  <s> 5 what are good quality settings for jpeg ? </s>  <s> most jpeg compressors let you pick a file size vs . </s>  <s> image quality tradeoff by selecting a quality setting . </s>  <s> there seems to be widespread confusion about the meaning of these settings . </s>  <s> quality 95 does not mean keep 95 of the information , as some have claimed . </s>  <s> the quality scale is purely arbitrary it s not a percentage of anything . </s>  <s> the name of the game in using jpeg is to pick the lowest quality setting smallest file size that decompresses into an image indistinguishable from the original . </s>  <s> this setting will vary from one image to another and from one observer to another , but here are some rules of thumb . </s>  <s> the default quality setting q 75 is very often the best choice . </s>  <s> this setting is about the lowest you can go without expecting to see defects in a typical image . </s>  <s> try q 75 first if you see defects , then go up . </s>  <s> except for experimental purposes , never go above q 95 saying q 100 will produce a file two or three times as large as q 95 , but of hardly any better quality . </s>  <s> if the image was less than perfect quality to begin with , you might be able to go down to q 50 without objectionable degradation . </s>  <s> on the other hand , you might need to go to a higher quality setting to avoid further degradation . </s>  <s> the second case seems to apply much of the time when converting gifs to jpeg . </s>  <s> the default q 75 is about right for compressing 24 bit images , but q 85 to 95 is usually better for converting gifs see section 14 for more info . </s>  <s> if you want a very small file say for preview or indexing purposes and are prepared to tolerate large defects , a q setting in the range of 5 to 10 is about right . </s>  <s> q 2 or so may be amusing as op art . </s>  <s> note the quality settings discussed in this article apply to the free jpeg software described in section 6b , and to many programs based on it . </s>  <s> other jpeg implementations , such as image alchemy , may use a completely different quality scale . </s>  <s> some programs don t even provide a numeric scale , just high medium low style choices . </s>  <s> 6 where can I get jpeg software ? </s>  <s> most of the programs described in this section are available by ftp . </s>  <s> if you don t know how to use ftp , see the faq article how to find sources . </s>  <s> if you don t have direct access to ftp , read about ftpmail servers in the same article . </s>  <s> that article appears regularly in news.answers , or you can get it by sending e mail to with send usenet news.answers finding sources in the body . </s>  <s> the anonymous ftp list faq may also be helpful it s usenet news.answers ftp list faq in the news.answers archive . </s>  <s> note this list changes constantly . </s>  <s> if you have a copy more than a couple months old , get the latest jpeg faq from the news.answers archive . </s>  <s> 6a if you are looking for canned software , viewers , etc the first part of this list is system specific programs that only run on one kind of system . </s>  <s> if you don t see what you want for your machine , check out the portable jpeg software described at the end of the list . </s>  <s> note that this list concentrates on free and shareware programs that you can obtain over internet but some commercial programs are listed too . </s>  <s> x windows xv shareware , 25 is an excellent viewer for jpeg , gif , and many other image formats . </s>  <s> it can also do format conversion and some simple image manipulations . </s>  <s> it s available for ftp from export.lcs.mit.edu 18.24 . </s>  <s> 0.12 , file contrib xv 3.00.tar . </s>  <s> z . </s>  <s> version 3.00 is a major upgrade with support for 24 bit displays and many other improvements however , it is brand new and still has some bugs lurking . </s>  <s> if you prefer not to be on the bleeding edge , stick with version 2.21 , also available from export . </s>  <s> note that version 2.21 is not a good choice if you have a 24 bit display you ll get only 8 bit color , nor for converting 24 bit images to jpeg . </s>  <s> but 2.21 works fine for converting gif and other 8 bit images to jpeg . </s>  <s> caution there is a glitch in version 2.21 be sure to check the save at normal size checkbox when saving a jpeg file , or the file will be blurry . </s>  <s> another good choice for x windows is john cristy s free imagemagick package , also available from export.lcs.mit.edu , file contrib imagemagick.tar . </s>  <s> z . </s>  <s> this package handles many image processing and conversion tasks . </s>  <s> the imagemagick viewer handles 24 bit displays correctly for colormapped displays , it does better though slower color quantization than xv or the basic free jpeg software . </s>  <s> both of the above are large , complex packages . </s>  <s> if you just want a simple image viewer , try xloadimage or xli . </s>  <s> xloadimage supports jpeg in its latest release , 3.03 . </s>  <s> xloadimage is free and available from export.lcs.mit.edu , file contrib xloadimage 3.03.tar . </s>  <s> z . </s>  <s> xli is a variant version of xloadimage , said by its fans to be somewhat faster and more robust than the original . </s>  <s> the current xli is indeed faster and more robust than the current xloadimage , at least with respect to jpeg files , because it has the ijg v4 decoder while xloadimage 3.03 is using a hacked over v1 . </s>  <s> the next xloadimage release will fix this . </s>  <s> xli is also free and available from export.lcs.mit.edu , file contrib xli.1.14.tar . </s>  <s> z . </s>  <s> both programs are said to do the right thing with 24 bit displays . </s>  <s> ms dos this covers plain dos for windows or os 2 programs , see the next headings . </s>  <s> one good choice is eric praetzel s free dvpeg , which views jpeg and gif files . </s>  <s> the current version , 2.5 , is available by ftp from sunee.uwaterloo.ca 129.97 . </s>  <s> 50.50 , file pub jpeg viewers dvpeg25.zip . </s>  <s> this is a good basic viewer that works on either 286 or 386 486 machines . </s>  <s> the user interface is not flashy , but it s functional . </s>  <s> another freeware jpeg gif tga viewer is mohammad rezaei s hiview . </s>  <s> the current version , 1.2 , is available from simtel 20 and mirror sites see note below , file msdos graphics hv12.zip . </s>  <s> hiview requires a 386 or better cpu and a vcpi compatible memory manager qemm 386 and 386max work windows and os 2 do not . </s>  <s> hiview is currently the fastest viewer for images that are no bigger than your screen . </s>  <s> for larger images , it scales the image down to fit on the screen rather than using panning scrolling as most viewers do . </s>  <s> you may or may not prefer this approach , but there s no denying that it slows down loading of large images considerably . </s>  <s> note installation is a bit tricky read the directions carefully ! </s>  <s> a shareware alternative is colorview for dos 30 . </s>  <s> this is easier to install than either of the two freeware alternatives . </s>  <s> its user interface is also much spiffier looking , although personally I find it harder to use more keystrokes , inconsistent behavior . </s>  <s> it is faster than dvpeg but a little slower than hiview , at least on my hardware . </s>  <s> for images larger than screen size , dvpeg and colorview seem to be about the same speed , and both are faster than hiview . </s>  <s> the current version is 2.1 , available from simtel 20 and mirror sites see note below , file msdos graphics dcview21.zip . </s>  <s> requires a vesa graphics driver if you don t have one , look in vesadrv2.zip or vesa tsr.zip from the same directory . </s>  <s> many recent pcs have a built in vesa driver , so don t try to load a vesa driver unless colorview complains that the driver is missing . </s>  <s> a second shareware alternative is fullview , which has been kicking around the net for a while , but I don t know any stable archive location for it . </s>  <s> the current rather old version is inferior to the above viewers anyway . </s>  <s> the author tells me that a new version of fullview will be out shortly and it will be submitted to the simtel 20 archives at that time . </s>  <s> the well known gif viewer compushow cshow supports jpeg in its latest revision , 8.60 a . </s>  <s> however , cshow s jpeg implementation isn t very good it s slow about half the speed of the above viewers and image quality is poor except on hi color displays . </s>  <s> too bad ... it d have been nice to see a good jpeg capability in cshow . </s>  <s> shareware , 25 . </s>  <s> available from simtel 20 and mirror sites see note below , file msdos gif cshw860a.zip . </s>  <s> due to the remarkable variety of pc graphics hardware , any one of these viewers might not work on your particular machine . </s>  <s> if you can t get any of them to work , you ll need to use one of the following conversion programs to convert jpeg to gif , then view with your favorite gif viewer . </s>  <s> if you have hi color hardware , don t use gif as the intermediate format try to find a targa capable viewer instead . </s>  <s> vpic 5.0 is reputed to do the right thing with hi color displays . </s>  <s> the independent jpeg group s free jpeg converters are ftpable from simtel 20 and mirror sites see note below , file msdos graphics jpeg4.zip or jpeg4386.zip if you have a 386 and extended memory . </s>  <s> these files are dos compilations of the free source code described in section 6b they will convert jpeg to and from gif , targa , and ppm formats . </s>  <s> handmade software offers free jpeg gif conversion tools , gif 2jpg jpg 2gif . </s>  <s> these are slow and are limited to conversion to and from gif format in particular , you can t get 24 bit color output from a jpeg . </s>  <s> the major advantage of these tools is that they will read and write hsi s proprietary jpeg format as well as the usenet standard jfif format . </s>  <s> since hsi format files are rather widespread on bbses , this is a useful capability . </s>  <s> version 2.0 of these tools is free prior versions were shareware . </s>  <s> get it from simtel 20 and mirror sites see note below , file msdos graphics gif2jpg2.zip . </s>  <s> note do not use hsi format for files to be posted on internet , since it is not readable on non pc platforms . </s>  <s> handmade software also has a shareware image conversion and manipulation package , image alchemy . </s>  <s> this will translate jpeg files both jfif and hsi formats to and from many other image formats . </s>  <s> it can also display images . view gifs . </s>  <s> jview also lacks some other useful features of the shareware viewers such as brightness adjustment , but it s an excellent basic viewer . </s>  <s> the current version , 0.9 , is quicktime system extension so you need to have quicktime installed . </s>  <s> to use quicktime , you need a 68020 or better cpu and you need to be running system 6.0 . </s>  <s> 7 or later . </s>  <s> if you re running system 6 , you must also install the 32 bit quickdraw extension this is built in on system 7 . </s>  <s> you can get quicktime by ftp from ftp.apple.com , file dts mac quicktime quicktime.hqx . </s>  <s> as of 11 92 , this file contains quicktime 1.5 , which is better than qt 1.0 in several ways . </s>  <s> with respect to jpeg , it is marginally faster and considerably less prone to crash when fed a corrupt jpeg file . </s>  <s> however , some applications seem to have compatibility problems with qt 1.5 . </s>  <s> mac users should keep in mind that quicktime s jpeg format , pict jpeg , is not the same as the usenet standard jfif jpeg format . </s>  <s> see section 10 for details . </s>  <s> if you post images on usenet , make sure they are in jfif format . </s>  <s> most of the programs mentioned below can generate either format . </s>  <s> the first choice is probably jpegview , a free program for viewing images that are in jfif format , pict jpeg format , or gif format . </s>  <s> it also can convert between the two jpeg formats . </s>  <s> the current version , 2.0 , is a big improvement over prior versions . </s>  <s> get it from sumex aim.stanford.edu 36.44 . </s>  <s> 0.6 , file info mac app jpeg view 20.hqx . </s>  <s> requires system 7 and quicktime . </s>  <s> on 8 bit displays , jpegview usually produces the best color image quality of all the currently available mac jpeg viewers . </s>  <s> jpegview can view large images in much less memory than other mac viewers in fact , it s the only one that can deal with jpeg images much over 640x480 pixels on a typical 4mb mac . </s>  <s> given a large image , jpegview automatically scales it down to fit on the screen , rather than presenting scroll bars like most other viewers . </s>  <s> you can zoom in on any desired portion , though . </s>  <s> some people like this behavior , some don t . </s>  <s> overall , jpegview s user interface is very well thought out . </s>  <s> gifconverter , a shareware 40 image viewer converter , supports jfif and pict jpeg , as well as gif and several other image formats . </s>  <s> the latest version is 2.3 . </s>  <s> 2 . </s>  <s> get it from sumex aim.stanford.edu , file info mac art gif gif converter 232.hqx . </s>  <s> requires system 6.0 . </s>  <s> 5 or later . </s>  <s> gifconverter is not better than jpegview as a plain jpeg
